{"code":1,"isDone":false,"toInsertArticleList":[{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"8 Best Ecommerce Marketing Strategies to Boost Your Sales and Revenue","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113372","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"1024\" height=\"683\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/s-o-c-i-a-l-c-u-t-eXmrW9I1Fnw-unsplash-1024x683.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">Operating an eCommerce site is not easy, and marketing it is a different game altogether. It requires you to put a lot of smart work and hard work in place to make any sizable income.</p> \n<p>But if you are aware of some robust marketing strategies that almost always deliver the results, your job can become a bit easier, and you can gain many customers easily. We know this, so we are going to share our knowledge and experience with you. In this article, we will introduce you with eight best eCommerce marketing strategies you can implement to boost your sales. Let us get started!</p> \n<h2>1. Utilize the power of Google Shopping Ads</h2> \n<p>In today’s time, there can be no better place to get your visitors than Google. The traffic coming from it converts more than any other traffic source, and it is also quite cheaper than the traffic from other marketing channels. However, the ranking will take time in Google’s search results. If you do not have that much patience, you can harness the power of Google Shopping Ads that appear on the top of the search pages whenever someone searches for a product. They look something like this:<br /></p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/unnamed-2.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113373\" />\n</figure> \n<p>As you can see, these ads not only allow you to occupy the top of a search results page but also will enable you to hook your visitors by showing a price, an image, and other relevant information right there on the search page itself. So, whoever visits your site by clicking these ads is more likely to convert into a customer, and you pay only when they click – which means a very high return on investment.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>2. Use SML (schema mark-up)</h2> \n<p>SML stands for Structured Mark-up Language. This language, also known popularly as Schema, helps search engines in better crawling and understanding of your site. By adding SML to your product pages, you can ensure that they are crawled and indexed correctly by Google and other search engines. While&nbsp;it doesn’t directly impact your search rankings, it does so indirectly by making your pages appear with information-rich snippets that entice people to click on your link instead of other links. And when that happens, it increases your Click-Through-Rate (CTR), which is an important ranking signal used by Google in its algorithms. As a result, you start moving up in search results from a steady pace.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>3. Upsell your products</h2> \n<p>In case you are not aware of it, upselling refers to selling a more premium or better version of your product than the customer is willing to buy. By doing this, you can increase your revenue without necessarily acquiring new customers, and that is precisely what makes this strategy cool. The strategy works because many times; the customer is not fully aware of what options – better or worse – are available in the market other than the product that (s)he is going to buy. If you can offer a better deal on your product pages by upselling relevant products, it can become a win-win situation for both you and your customers.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>4. Protect your site with an SSL certificate&nbsp;</h2> \n<p>Since we are about security, it is also important to discuss another security-related element that can turn visitors away from your site if it appears. If your website lacks an SSL certificate and therefore loading over default HTTP protocol instead of the more secure HTTPS, web browsers show a&nbsp;<em>“Not Secure”</em>&nbsp;label before your URL in the address bar. Something like this:</p> \n<p>You can imagine what such a label appearing before your URL can do damage to your brand. The visitors to your site will feel that something is seriously wrong with the security of your website (which would also be true, given the importance of SSL) and immediately hit that dreaded Close Tab button. If you want to ensure that it does not happen, install an SSL certificate on your site. In case you are clueless about which certificate to buy,&nbsp;there are many SSL certificates out there in the market like Comodo certificate, DigiCert certificate, <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuY2xpY2tzc2wubmV0L2dlb3RydXN0LXNzbC1jZXJ0aWZpY2F0ZXMtYXV0aG9yaXplZC1yZXNlbGxlcg%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113372\"><strong>GeoTrust SSL certificates</strong></a>&nbsp;are among the best ones in the industry.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>5. Pay attention to site speed</h2> \n<p>The speed of your site matters a lot when you are selling something. Nobody likes waiting nowadays – especially if they are looking to purchase something. If your site is slow to load, they will close it and want to buy from somewhere else. Do not let that happen – increase your site speed by following the steps outlined below:</p> \n<p>Enable caching on your site.</p> \n<ul>\n <li>Eliminate unnecessary elements from your product pages (i.e., excess javascript/CSS, images/media loading from external sources, multiple widgets, etc.)</li>\n <li>Choose a reliable web hosting company</li>\n <li>Check your site with&nbsp;the Google Page Speed Insights&nbsp;tool and implement the steps suggested to boost your Page Speed score.</li>\n <li>These steps can help you enough in ensuring that your site loads faster.&nbsp;</li>\n</ul> \n<h2>6. Leverage email marketing</h2> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuam90Zm9ybS5jb20vZW1haWwtbWFya2V0aW5nLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113372\">Email marketing</a> may sound like an old technique in an all-social media-driven world. However, it still works wonders for many businesses. Especially if you are running an eCommerce business, you can leverage its power in many ways. You can start a blog that sends customers to your product pages after they’re educated enough to purchase your product, you can also use email addresses of your users to inform them about a product that was out of stock as soon as it’s back in stock. Last, but certainly not least, you can also tell your customers about various sales offers you are running through emails.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>7. Use Trust Seals on your checkout page</h2> \n<p>Often when people do not buy from your site, it is not something wrong with your marketing, but with the security, elements included, or not included in your website.&nbsp;<a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuY2xpY2tzc2wubmV0L2Jsb2cvYmlnZ2VzdC1zZWN1cml0eS10aHJlYXRzLWZvci1hbi1vbmxpbmUtYnVzaW5lc3M%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113372\"><strong>Security threats for an online business</strong></a>&nbsp;are among the top concerns in your mind and in the minds of your potential customers, which is why they do not purchase from sites that do not make them feel safe. If you want to make your visitors feel safe on your website, include some Trust Seals from reputed brands on your site (especially your checkout page), as shown above. You will need to purchase some security-related products from these brands to display these seals, but that is worth it because it will also boost your sales revenue.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>8. Use videos in your product pages and marketing strategy</h2> \n<p>Finally, use the power of video to improve your product pages and boost your marketing. On product pages, videos can be used to provide your customers with a better understanding of the product they are buying. Off the product page, they can be used as a marketing tool to send visitors to your site through video sharing platforms like YouTube and other social media channels. It would help if you crafted a solid marketing strategy around it, and you can drive tons of traffic and sales to your eCommerce site through this one marketing medium alone.&nbsp;</p> \n<h4><strong>Conclusion</strong></h4> \n<p>So, these were eight best eCommerce marketing strategies you must implement to boost your sales. It is easy to implement them and necessary because, without these strategies, you cannot get the best ROI out of your marketing campaigns. Please share your thoughts and <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/constructive-feedback.html\">feedback</a> about them in the comments below and let us know how they perform for your site. </p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<p><em>Photo by </em><a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly91bnNwbGFzaC5jb20vQHNvY2lhbGN1dD91dG1fc291cmNlPXVuc3BsYXNoJmFtcDt1dG1fbWVkaXVtPXJlZmVycmFsJmFtcDt1dG1fY29udGVudD1jcmVkaXRDb3B5VGV4dA%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113372\"><em>S O C I A L . marketing</a> is a vital tool for businesses because it instils a level of confidence in a brand by demonstrating expertise, trustworthiness and authority on relevant topics as well as satisfying search needs. </p> \n<p>This can help to win sales and conversions alike as well as earning valuable backlinks from high-quality websites.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>As an online learning platform, your business could significantly benefit from the power of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/how-to-use-design-to-amplify-your-brands-content-marketing.html\">content marketing</a> and search engine optimisation efforts. This is down to the level of confidence that visitors will need prior to enrolling with you or signing up for more information.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>With this in mind, let’s take a deeper look into the relationship between content and digital education organisations. Here are five key reasons why quality content is key to the success of online learning platforms:</p> \n<h3><strong>Demonstrate Your Credibility</strong></h3> \n<p>When it comes to online learning, one of the most significant ways of building conversions is through demonstrating your credibility.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Online courses, in particular, can be significantly time-consuming and demanding challenges for users, and it’s of the utmost importance that they know their efforts will be rewarded with a recognisable qualification in return for their hard work.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>To entrust you with their contact information (not to mention bank details), visitors will <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9hbmljY2EuY28udWsvYmxvZy8xMi1yZWFzb25zLXdoeS1jb250ZW50LW1hcmtldGluZy1pcy1hbi1pbXBvcnRhbnQtcGFydC1vZi15b3VyLW1hcmtldGluZy1taXgv&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113098\">need to have confidence in your platform’s credibility</a>.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>By <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9zb2x2aWQuY28udWsvaG93LXRvLXN0YXJ0LWEtYmxvZy8%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113098\">creating content for an on-site blog or news feed</a>, you have a large canvas in which to not only build keywords and backlinks but to also build trust in your services and forge some levels of confidence in your platform.</p> \n<p>Content marketing can influence users by showing that your education website is well run and possesses a great deal of industry expertise.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>It’s also possible to make content from testimonials and product reviews as a means of getting the message across that your company is a great choice for customers.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The topic of education is a tricky one to demonstrate credibility in. While pass rates and satisfaction scores can help to show that your courses are successful, it’s only from content that interested visitors will gain a better understanding of exactly what you’re offering.</p> \n<h3><strong>Make Your Platform Visible</strong></h3> \n<p>Content gets you noticed. Search engine optimisation forms the cornerstone to great content and carries the power to drive traffic to your website as well as high-quality do-follow backlinks.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Primarily, your learning platform needs to be visible to the right audiences at the right time. Because so many users look to Google to find the things they’re looking for online, it can be easy to create content that utilises searchable keywords.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Simply speaking, if you can build articles that use the right blend of keywords and on-page SEO, you can make your platform much more visible at the top of Google’s results pages, as opposed to vying for space among rival organisations with advertising campaigns.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The best thing about optimising your content is that it can create a steady stream of traffic over time, rather than the more short-term approaches of PPC advertising campaigns.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>Generate Awareness</strong></h3> \n<p>Creating awareness of your organisation and brand can run up expensive PR bills. Content marketing, however, could be significantly more cost-efficient and every bit as expensive for your target audiences.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Here, it could be written content, video-based insights into your office environment, or copy optimised for social media, as long as it helps potential customers to feel more familiar with your company it can be a great asset.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>When you produce on-site content, always make sure you talk of your business as if it were a living organism, as opposed to conveying yourself as an independent author. Readers can identify with a personable approach and build a level of trust in your organisation.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>While brand awareness isn’t typically easy for companies to actually quantify, it’s an integral goal for marketing departments to get some form of branding under the noses of target audiences in order to build familiarity. High-quality and engaging content is one of the most effective and non-intrusive ways of developing branding.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>Accommodate Niche Audiences</strong></h3> \n<p>The great thing about content is that it can appeal directly to your readers’ wants and needs. The better you know your target audience, the more specific your content can be in appealing to their motivations. While sales and service pages need to be appealing in a more general sense, content pieces can cherrypick specific talking points among groups that you’ve identified as among the most likely to enrol into your learning platform.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>It’s important to note that this approach requires a significant level of pre-planning and audience knowledge. If you can identify the needs of your target market, it should be down to your company to satisfy them through your content.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>It may seem counterintuitive to pigeonhole your content to appeal to niche audiences, but in this current age of saturated content and hyper-competitivity, it’s effective to step back from your goals and look at where you can fine-tune your approach.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>Call Your Visitors to Action</strong></h3> \n<p>Fundamentally, the most effective benefit that content has over other forms of marketing is the discreet way in which calls-to-action (CTAs) can be added to your copy.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>For an online learning platform, this is especially useful to encourage visitors to access further information or fill out sign-up forms.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The process of signing up to an online course can take a little time, so it’s vital that platforms can build enough levels of interest in visitors before asking if they’re willing to follow up on their interest online.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Be sure to supply your target audience with a healthy level of information and confidence-building copy before inviting them to sign up to a newsletter or share their email address for alerts.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Remember that online education involves plenty of effort and commitment for digital students. It’s only fair that online learning portals share the same level of enthusiasm. </p> \n<img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113098\" width=\"1\" height=\"1\" style=\"display: none;\" />","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Fri, 14 Aug 2020 14:51:31 +0000","feedId":2999,"bgimg":"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/nick-morrison-FHnnjk1Yj7Y-unsplash-1024x768.jpg","linkMd5":"6c619ccbd9ab959693e02259fc1567a4","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn14@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-38-127_2149a7647e923cfb.webp","destWidth":1024,"destHeight":768,"sourceBytes":327380,"destBytes":53962,"author":"Peter Jobes","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/nick-morrison-FHnnjk1Yj7Y-unsplash-1024x768.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn14@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-38-127_2149a7647e923cfb.webp","https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113098":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn62@2020_3/2020/08/24/15-51-46-175_fb2fadd04505c7b0.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598284297221},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"5 Steps to Improve Your Logo Design","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113294","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"1000\" height=\"471\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Untitled-1-3.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">As you move forward in your career, your logo designing skills should be honed as well if you keep practising it. However, to come up with something extraordinary, that would create a striking impression; simply practising is not enough.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Listed below are 5 steps that can help you improve your logo designing skills and <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2Rlc2lnbi9ob3ctdG8tZGVzaWduLWFuLWljb25pYy1sb2dvLmh0bWw%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113294\">create a logo</a> that leaves a lasting impression on the minds of your target audience.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>1. Conduct In-depth Research</strong></h3> \n<p><a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2Rlc2lnbi90aGUtZG9zLWFuZC1kb250cy1vZi1sb2dvLWRlc2lnbi5odG1s&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113294\">Logo design</a> is not about mixing and matching a few colours and making it look pretty. It may sound clichéd but a logo is the face of your brand and thus it should have all the correct elements that would click with the audience. Thus, in-depth research is extremely important. From your client to their brands and their competitors, as a logo designer, you need to keep your game up and see what you can do to come up with a dynamic logo or may improve their existing one.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Thorough research means that you understand the company and the brand and what it does. Similarly, you need to be aware of the competition as well. Research of all the related sources from their website to social media platforms, everything should come under your scrutiny. You must be wondering why to study social media platforms? Well, it is the best place to learn about the targeted audience and what they want from your client.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>2. Deep &amp; Probing Questions</strong></h3> \n<p>If you are working on your logo yourself or you have been asked to improve an existing logo of a brand, the second most important thing after the research is to ask deep and probing questions that would help you create their <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9mdWxsc3RvcDM2MC5jb20vbG9nby1kZXNpZ24%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113294\">custom logo</a>. Probe deeply and find out the vision behind the brand and what exactly do the leaders in the company perceive about it.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>From the target audience to the ideas for growing the business, you need to ask everything. Ask about the brand’s competition, long-term goals and even if some questions seem irrelevant, it is essential that you ask the questions anyway as it will only add to the improvement in designing a custom logo.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>3. Mobile-Oriented</strong></h3> \n<p>The third most important step when it comes to logo designing or tweaking is; that it should be customized for the mobile phones. Whether you are designing a logo from scratch or improvising an old one, both should be customized according to the requirements of the mobile phones. When you are conducting the research, you will realize that many companies have simplified and flattened their logos to make it easier to see on the mobile screens. From Facebook, Instagram, Microsoft and eBay and many more have adopted this strategy and <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2Rlc2lnbi9kZXNpZ24tdGlwcy15b3UtY2FuLXVzZS10by1lbWJyYWNlLW1pbmltYWxpc3QtbWFya2V0aW5nLWRlc2lnbi5odG1s&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113294\">minimalized</a> their logos.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The reason behind all tech giants adopting this element is that mobile phones have become more popular for online navigation than desktops and laptops and too complex designs can lose their impact on the mini-screens of cell-phones. To keep the logo recognizable, it is of utmost importance to keep the logo identifiable and minimal for the small mobile screen.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>4. Step Out from Comfort Zone</strong></h3> \n<p>Want to phenomenally improve your <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/design/the-dos-and-donts-of-logo-design.html\">logo design</a> or polish up your skills to an extraordinary level? Then, the font that you use can make all the difference. A unique and distinctive font can become your brand’s identity and set it apart from the competition. Take the example of the Harry Potter franchise. The unique font that was introduced in the first Harry Potter movie more than twenty years ago is a trademark for the brand. The audience automatically associates that particular font with everything that has to do with HP franchise. New fonts are being introduced every now and then, and you can also find one that really identifies with the brand you are working on.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>If you think that you will have to pay for the new fonts, then it is a misconception. With tools like <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuYWRvYmUuY29tL3RyL3Byb2R1Y3RzL2lsbHVzdHJhdG9yLmh0bWw%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113294\">Adobe Illustrator</a>, you can tinker with various font styles without having to spend money on them. Some others even offer trial services before you purchase the actual thing. So, go ahead and experiment with fonts for some inspiration. You don’t have to necessarily spend a lot of money to take advantage of new fonts, either.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3><strong>5. Study the Maestros</strong></h3> \n<p>When you go online, there is myriad of logo designs and there are galleries full of it. However, not all these designs are done by gurus in the field. In fact most of them are the creation of students and amateur designers. To get true inspiration, you must study the maestros in the field and only then will you be able to improve your logo design.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>When it some to learning, do not compromise; learn from the most phenomenal maestros in the field – the big brand logos. Don’t settle for less than the best when it comes to logo designs and get your inspiration from those who have managed to persist even after the arrival of all the new technology.&nbsp;Whatever you do, you need to remember that when it comes to log design, your targeted audience will never pay attention to its minute details. On the contrary, they will just glance at it for milliseconds and that’s the time you have to make an impression. Keeping your designs minimal yet impactful, it needs to touch a chord with the subconscious human instincts at their most primal level. Whatever you do, always design or improvise the designs keeping the human audience in mind. They are no experts of all the intricacies in your design. They need to connect with the brand on a psychological level with a few milliseconds.</p> \n<p>This is what you can see when it comes to the logos of famous brands like Nike, Coca-Cola, McDonald’s or even the tri-petal design of Adidas. Simply put, try to understand the psychology of the audience you are targeting and you will be able to establish yourself as an extraordinary logo designer and improve your logo designs phenomenally.&nbsp;</p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<p>Photo by <a 23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"4 Essential Ways to Check Your Website’s Health","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113280","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"1000\" height=\"471\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Untitled-1-2.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">Many website owners falsely think that their websites are going to work perfectly forever. However, in reality, all websites eventually break.</p> \n<p>This happens because sites are running out of date, plugins stop working, or as a result of a cyberattack. If you want to avoid these issues altogether, the solution is rooted in regular digital health checks. In this article, I’ll focus on the simple and inexpensive website health check ways that will help your website run flawlessly!&nbsp;</p> \n<h2><strong>What is a website health check and why do you need one?&nbsp;</strong></h2> \n<p>A website health check implies breaking down the anatomy of your website to evaluate the functionality, performance, and design of your web pages. Here’s why it’s important to conduct regular website health checks.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Any change that you make on your pages somehow affects the overall health of your site. Let’s say, you’ve decided to add a second Spanish version of your website. This can influence the speed and overall performance of your site. That’s why designing and implementing a regular website maintenance check is an absolute must.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Not particularly sure where to begin your site’s health check? No worries, we’ve got you covered. Here’s a list of the four essential factors to make sure your website is healthy.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3>1. <strong>Performance testing&nbsp;</strong></h3> \n<p>Did you know that <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cudGhpbmt3aXRoZ29vZ2xlLmNvbS9tYXJrZXRpbmctcmVzb3VyY2VzL2RhdGEtbWVhc3VyZW1lbnQvbW9iaWxlLXBhZ2Utc3BlZWQtbmV3LWluZHVzdHJ5LWJlbmNobWFya3Mv&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113280\">53% of users</a> will leave your website if it doesn’t load within 3 seconds? Moreover, studies show that website speed directly impacts business’ profitability.&nbsp;</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image4-2.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113281\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Image Source: </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9zdG9yYWdlLmdvb2dsZWFwaXMuY29tL3R3Zy1jb250ZW50L29yaWdpbmFsX2ltYWdlcy9tb2JpbGUtcGFnZS1zcGVlZC1uZXctaW5kdXN0cnktYmVuY2htYXJrcy0wMS0yMS5wbmc%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113280\"><em>https://storage.googleapis.com/twg-content/original_images/mobile-page-speed-new-industry-benchmarks-01-21.png</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<p>This way, your website’s speed and performance are the key factors contributing to the revenue generated and your overall success.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Performance testing is considered a part of a website’s health check and one of the most challenging testings. Performance testing is executed to test the responsiveness, speed, scalability, and throughput of your website.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>There are many ways to carry out performance testing. For example, you can use dedicated online tools and browser extensions.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3>2. <strong>SEO testing&nbsp;</strong></h3> \n<p>Search engine optimization (SEO) is another important aspect of your website. Your site’s ranking and discoverability in search engines can play a major role in the overall success of your website and your business in general. That’s why you want to ensure your SEO is in place as a part of the website health check.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Regular SEO testing will help you identify the best SEO tactics for your business. In the meantime, simple SEO practices will help you keep your site healthy. For example, by regularly updating your web pages and images, you can boost your ranking on Google and get rid of the outdated content.&nbsp;<br /></p> \n<h3>3. <strong>Security checking&nbsp;</strong></h3> \n<p>As more businesses are operating online, there is a growing threat of cyberattacks. In fact, <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuYWNjZW50dXJlLmNvbS9fYWNubWVkaWEvUERGLTk2L0FjY2VudHVyZS0yMDE5LUNvc3Qtb2YtQ3liZXJjcmltZS1TdHVkeS1GaW5hbC5wZGYjem9vbT01MA%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113280\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">studies show</a> that 68% of business leaders feel that cybersecurity risks are increasing. That’s why ensuring security is a crucial step towards a healthier website.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> \n<p>As much as we all rely on the web, it’s not exactly the safest place. Your website may be exposed to cyberattacks by accident or by mistake. For example, you can install a plugin without even knowing that it’s carrying malware. In the meantime, the faulty plugin is infecting your website and puts the entire system at risk.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>To keep your website safe and keep off cybercriminals, you need to check and update your website regularly. Use website security checking tools that can enable you to do the following:</p> \n<ul>\n <li>Detect viruses and malware</li>\n <li>Detect phishing attacks, ActiveX attacks, buffer overflow, and other vulnerabilities&nbsp;&nbsp;</li>\n <li>Check user IPs against various spammer databases&nbsp;</li>\n <li>Detect whether or not your SSL certificate expires soon</li>\n <li>Manage regular website updates&nbsp;</li>\n</ul> \n<h3>4. <strong>Broken links testing</strong></h3> \n<p>Besides performance, SEO, and security checking, there is another aspect commonly overlooked when checking website health – links.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The web consists of a plethora of links that are used to locate and connect pieces of information. A single website can have hundreds and even thousands of links. However, when these links become broken, it will affect your website’s speed and overall performance.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Links do so much more than just sending users to your website. They are accountable for displaying graphics, data, and various applications.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Here’s a list of links you should keep an eye for when checking your website health:&nbsp;</p> \n<ul>\n <li>External links to other websites&nbsp;</li>\n <li>Internal links to your images&nbsp;</li>\n <li>Internal links to pages&nbsp;</li>\n</ul> \n<h3><strong>Tools for website health checks&nbsp;</strong></h3> \n<p>Gathering required information that can show you the problem areas is the first step of the website health checking. Once all of the needed data has been collected, the next step is to take the required actions to fix the problems.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Here are some tools you can use to check your website’s health.&nbsp;</p> \n<h4><strong>Google Search Console&nbsp;</strong></h4> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image1-2-1024x576.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113282\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Image Source: </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9nbGltcHNlLm1lZGlhL3dwLWNvbnRlbnQvdXBsb2Fkcy8yMDIwLzA0L2dvb2dsZS1zZWFyY2gtY29uc29sZS1sb2dvLTEyMDB4Njc1LnBuZw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113280\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\"><em>https://glimpse.media/wp-content/uploads/2020/04/google-search-console-logo-1200×675.png</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<p>Google Search Console is a free tool that helps you monitor, maintain, improve your website’s presence in Google Search results. Since there are no clear guidelines on how Google’s ranking algorithms work, Google Search Console is an invaluable tool that can help you understand and advance how Google sees your website.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Google Search Console allows you to troubleshoot the following issues:</p> \n<ul>\n <li>XML sitemap errors</li>\n <li>Structured data errors&nbsp;</li>\n <li>Broken links&nbsp;</li>\n <li>Robots.txt errors&nbsp;</li>\n <li>Mobile usability issues&nbsp;</li>\n</ul> \n<h4><strong>PageSpeed Insights&nbsp;</strong></h4> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image3-4.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113283\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Image Source: </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9oc3RvLm9yZy93ZWJ0L3RmL2wwL25hL3RmbDBuYWs2dHVid2J5YWpkZW8tZHBxamFzMC5wbmc%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113280\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\"><em>https://hsto.org/webt/tf/l0/na/tfl0nak6tubwbyajdeo-dpqjas0.png</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<p>Google PageSpeed Insights is another free tool that allows you to check the page speed of your website. Besides, it shows you various factors affecting the speed, so you know what needs adjustment.&nbsp;</p> \n<h4><strong>Ahrefs&nbsp;</strong></h4> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image2-3.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113284\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Image Source: </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly90ZW1wbGF0ZXRlc3Rlci5jb20vd3AtY29udGVudC91cGxvYWRzLzIwMjAvMDEvYWhyZWZzLWxvZ28tMy5wbmc%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113280\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\"><em>https://templatetester.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/01/ahrefs-logo-3.png</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<p>Ahrefs is an SEO toolset that can help you monitor the status of your backlinks and referring domains. The tool enables you to record the number of backlinks and referring domains gained, broken, or lost. This way, you can contact the website to identify and solve the problem with backlinks.&nbsp;</p> \n<p><strong>Wrapping it up!&nbsp;</strong></p> \n<p>When you <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly96eXJvLmNvbS93ZWJzaXRl&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113280\">build a pro website</a>, it’s important to keep it updated and conduct regular website health checks. Essentially, you have to follow a two-step process that includes collecting all health-check tools and then implementing required fixes.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Before you go, let’s quickly wrap up what you’ve learned today about the four essential ways to check your website’s health:&nbsp;</p> \n<ol>\n <li>Performance testing is a fundamental part of any website health check and includes testing the website’s responsiveness, speed, scalability, and throughput.&nbsp;</li>\n <li>SEO testing allows you to monitor the status of your site and improve ranking.&nbsp;</li>\n <li>Regular security checking can help you identify and troubleshoot malicious threats to your site.</li>\n <li>Broken links testing allows you to find faulty links and keep your website updated.&nbsp;</li>\n</ol> \n<p>Keeping your website healthy doesn’t have to be rocket science. The key ingredient lies in regular health checks. By following these four practices and using dedicated tools, you can take it a step further and ensure your website’s health at all times!&nbsp;</p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<p><a Falk","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Untitled-1-2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn70@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-38-061_48e9f995281b05af.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image4-2.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn85@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-46-390_ff8fd8b44eb7d095.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image1-2-1024x576.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn93@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-45-741_4a93b18ae3a99982.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image3-4.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx6/cdn22@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-47-221_df548c1cd89b4a04.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image2-3.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn58@2020_2/2020/08/24/15-51-47-594_c001636a916f95d4.webp","https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113280":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn97@2020_2/2020/08/24/15-51-45-612_5fb6671a205a7d00.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598284297213},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"6 Best Video Editing Tips Every Graphic Designer Should Know","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113329","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"1024\" height=\"683\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/pexels-kelly-lacy-4041405-1024x683.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">After you give your blood, sweat, and tears filming the video and already get the footage you need, it’s time for the other half of the battle: the editing process.</p> \n<p>This process is where all those footages you have molded into a story. In this matter, you can say that smooth video editing is much more than just straight cutting. It’s creating an enticing story and vision.</p> \n<p>When it comes to video editing, you don’t need a master’s film degree to be an editor. Even if you’re a graphic designer, you can still sit in the editing room, working with the directors and sound engineers.</p> \n<p>Whatever your background is, there are some pretty definitive ‘rules’ that you should stick to in order to get the videos right. Get them wrong, and your videos end up looking very flat and boring, making them look unprofessional.</p> \n<p>Below are some basic <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9icmVhZG5iZXlvbmQuY29tL2FydGljbGVzL3ZpZGVvLWVkaXRpbmctdGlwcy8%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113329\">video editing tips</a>, especially for graphic designers, to produce the most enjoyable video for the viewers.</p> \n<h2>Graphic Designers and Video Editing: How It’s Related</h2> \n<p>But, before we get into the nitty-gritty, it’s important to understand why you can’t actually separate video editing and graphic design.</p> \n<p>Graphic designers and video editors might be two different professions, but they are short of interconnected with one another. Graphic design is all about creating images using the composition of colors, lines, textures, and shapes. Meanwhile, video editing is “designing” the video by creating a story using a combination of footage, color, typography, symbols, and more.</p> \n<p>It means that it’d be much helpful if you have design skills while editing videos. Those kinds of skills will help add value to your works and excel in your field, leading to more opportunities.</p> \n<h2>Video Editing Tips for Graphic Designers</h2> \n<p>Since films or videos are also very much designed in the same way that you design posters or brochures, we mostly focus on the editing tips that have a strong element of design.</p> \n<h3>1. Utilize the Best Video Designing Tools</h3> \n<p>Thanks to the internet — now you can easily use software and any other <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9icmVhZG5iZXlvbmQuY29tL3ZpZGVvLW1hcmtldGluZy90b29scy8%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113329\">video tools</a> you need to help you create well-edited, stunning videos. There is a bunch of software out there, and they basically offer you basic editing features for standard video edits.</p> \n<p>In this case, you can choose the right ones for you based on your preferences and needs. So, you need to pay attention to their usability, digital interface, and features. Make sure all of them match your editing capabilities and style.</p> \n<p>Some of the most popular <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/essentials/video-editing-software.html\">video editing software</a> are After Effects, Final Cut Pro, Premiere Pro, Adobe Premiere Pro, and more.</p> \n<h3>2. Master the Hotkeys</h3> \n<p>Keyboard shortcuts might sound nerdy. After all, you’re not an IT director that needs this thing the most.</p> \n<p>However, since video editing takes already long enough, you can speed up the process by mastering some keyboard shortcuts or hotkeys.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>These combinations of keys on the keyboard help you perform a certain task within a program faster and more comfortably than by using a mouse. In other words, it bridges the gap between effort and action, helping you save more time to move from point A to point B efficiently.</p> \n<p>What’s more, mastering hotkeys also allows you to fine-tune details in your audiovisual projects. Therefore, you can create a compelling video without taking too much time spent on the point-and-click method.</p> \n<h3>3. Think About Color Corrections</h3> \n<p>Color is such a crucial element when it comes to video graphics. It sets the mood and helps convey the overall message. And in most video production, even with the help of good light settings or excellent scenery conditions, the raw footage you have still tend to be over-saturated and bland at first.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Therefore, you need to balance them out with color corrections by adjusting the levels of particular colors within it — which every graphic designer has been dealing with.</p> \n<p>Color corrections help your final product to have a consistent color palette. It ensures that no detail is lost when your video is watched on the viewers’ screen.</p> \n<h3>4. Add Stunning Graphics and Effects</h3> \n<p>Graphics can make a bigger difference to your video production. In this case, there are many different types of graphics you can add to your video to make it more engaging and captivating.</p> \n<p>For instance, you can add motions to make the viewers more focus on the content. You can add logos to make great branding enhancements. You might also add some typography or titles to make it easier for viewers to digest the content.</p> \n<p>The key to adding graphics here is to help your audience to quickly recognize and seamlessly connect emotionally with you and your video.</p> \n<h3>5. Understand the Lingo</h3> \n<p>Just like any other industry, video editing has a language all its own. And one thing that can make your <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/what-is-workflow.html\">workflow</a> much easier is understanding that language. Remember, editing not only comprises “the cut” since there’s no single way to edit footage.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>In this situation, understanding video editing terms won’t only help you edit an astounding video and make it easier for you to communicate with other editors or clients.</p> \n<p>From transition to jump cut, learning the lingo and speaking the post-production team’s language can spark your creativity and improve your editing skills.</p> \n<h3>6. Strive for Clarity</h3> \n<p>Both design and editing are fundamentally about striving for clarity. So, even though it’s great to know a lot of editing techniques and design skills, it’s crucial to keep it clean and easy on the eye.</p> \n<p>More techniques applied to the editing process doesn’t always mean a better final result. Make sure you don’t go overboard with your editing. It will make your video chaotic, and the viewers will have a hard time understanding what you are talking about.</p> \n<p>Try to only add the elements that will improve your video and avoid using unnecessary ones. With clear and simple editing, the viewers are left in no doubt about what’s being discussed in the video.</p> \n<h4>Wrapping Up</h4> \n<p>Video editing is such a key process in production since it’s not all about stunning visuals, but it’s also about making the viewers feel emotionally connected. Your editing goal should always be to deliver an enticing story that can evoke your viewers’ emotions.</p> \n<p>Sometimes that means you need to break some industry standards to make your video unique and stand out among the rest. That’s why design skills can help you to improve the final results. With some design skills, you’d be able to edit videos and add the exact atmosphere that fits the videos’ content while also deliver valuable information. </p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/video-marketing-featured-1024x621.png\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" /> \n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">Content-based marketing has become the gold standard for boosting brand awareness, reaching customers, driving web traffic, and increasing the bottom line. But there’s one area of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/how-to-use-design-to-amplify-your-brands-content-marketing.html\">content marketing</a> that’s still in its infancy: video marketing.</p> \n<p>Interest in video content marketing has grown as people’s preferences shift toward this dynamic medium. Businesses have naturally responded by allocating a greater portion of their marketing budgets to exploring and taking advantage of video, using it across social media, in ads, and on company websites.</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"> \n  <img src=\"https://www.jotform.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/video-marketing-intro-02-700x544.png\" alt=\"video content marketing\" class=\"wp-image-295037\" /> \n </figure> \n</div> \n<p>In this guide, we walk through a number of video content marketing concepts, including defining the term and sharing benefits you can expect from video marketing. You’ll also learn about the types of videos you can produce, and even steps you can take to create a video marketing strategy of your own.</p> \n<h2>Chapter synopsis</h2> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Chapter 1: Introduction.</strong></li> \n <li><strong><a data-trigger=\"go-to-section\" data-target=\"292397\" title=\"What is video marketing?\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"javascript:;\">Chapter 2: What is video marketing?</a></strong> We start by covering the basics of video marketing, including its importance and how it’s being used in practice. We also provide some useful tips on creating videos that just might help you go viral.</li> \n <li><strong><a data-trigger=\"go-to-section\" data-target=\"292417\" title=\"Benefits of video marketing\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"javascript:;\">Chapter 3: Benefits of video marketing.</a></strong> What good things can you expect from starting video marketing in your business? Results vary, but many companies that go down this road experience greater brand awareness and several other advantages.</li> \n <li><strong><a data-trigger=\"go-to-section\" data-target=\"292487\" title=\"Types of videos\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"javascript:;\">Chapter 4: Types of videos.</a></strong> Videos are dynamic media, offering you a lot of creative flexibility, which is why there are several different types of video you can produce. In this chapter, we cover six of the most common ones businesses use today.</li> \n <li><strong><a data-trigger=\"go-to-section\" data-target=\"292537\" title=\"How to create a video marketing strategy\" rel=\"noopener noreferrer\" href=\"javascript:;\">Chapter 5: How to create a video marketing strategy.</a></strong> Put what you’ve learned in the previous chapters to work with expert guidance on creating a video marketing strategy of your own. You’ll walk away with concrete steps that can help your business stand out from the crowd.</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Remember to bookmark this guide for later reference. You never know when you may need to brush up on a few tips or try new types of videos you haven’t yet explored.</p> \n<h2>What is video marketing?</h2> \n<p>“They say a picture is worth a thousand words. But video allows you to say a lot more,” says Randall Harp, creator in chief at <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9jaGFwZWxoaWxsbWVkaWEuY29tLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">Chapel Hill Media</a>. This idea captures the sentiment behind<em> </em>video marketing.<em> </em>To be more concrete about it, video marketing is a modern content marketing tactic businesses use to generate interest in their products and services.</p> \n<p>Video marketing lets you communicate a lot more information to prospects and customers in less time than written content, and it helps audiences connect with your brand in a more engaging way.<strong> </strong>Below we answer a few questions to help solidify the concept of video marketing.</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"> \n  <img src=\"https://www.jotform.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/What-is-video-marketing-03-700x544.png\" alt=\"video marketing\" class=\"wp-image-295057\" /> \n </figure> \n</div> \n<h3>3 FAQs about video marketing</h3> \n<h4>Why video marketing?</h4> \n<p>Harp calls out two key reasons why video marketing has become such a popular tactic for marketers:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Culture shift.</strong> People tend to be visual, so it’s not surprising more people are choosing to watch instead of read since video is more commonplace today. <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cucHN5Y2hvbG9neXRvZGF5LmNvbS91cy9ibG9nL2dldC1wc3ljaGVkLzIwMTIwNy9sZWFybmluZy10aHJvdWdoLXZpc3VhbHM%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">Studies show</a> that people receive and remember information better when it’s visual. “Plus, we live in a fast-paced culture where we’re very conscious of time, and reading takes more of it. That’s why video is such a great way to reach people rather than expecting them to sit and consume pages of text,” he explains.</li> \n <li><strong>Technology.</strong> The ability to produce and consume video has become much easier thanks to easier-to-use creator tools, smartphones, and social media. “While high-quality, well-scripted videos are easier to make, not every video has to be a Hollywood production. You can use your smartphone to record, then quickly and easily upload it to any social platform,” he says.</li> \n</ul> \n<h4>How is video marketing being used?</h4> \n<p>While consumers tend to create videos for nonmonetary reasons, Harp notes that companies, of course, use video marketing to benefit their business. Specifically, they use it to</p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Sell products.</strong> Many businesses use popular social platforms like Instagram, which focuses on visuals, to showcase their products. These social posts can then help drive people to a brick-and-mortar store or send them directly to an online shopping site.</li> \n <li><strong>Increase brand awareness.</strong> Businesses can also use videos to promote their brand or corporate identity, though Harp says this is typically reserved for larger companies with equally large budgets — for example, Coca-Cola and Apple.</li> \n <li><strong>Share information.</strong> Today’s digital landscape has spawned a knowledge culture that’s willing to pay for information. People such as Instagram influencers and business coaches often capitalize on this by engaging with viewers through videos and live streaming to create a following of people who may eventually convert to customers — purchasing courses, diet and exercise plans, sales training, and so on.</li> \n <li><strong>Promote company culture.</strong> From a different perspective, businesses also use video marketing to attract new talent. By giving prospective employees a look behind the scenes, businesses can open the door to their company culture and spur a desire to work there.</li> \n</ul> \n<h4>Tips for getting started with video marketing</h4> \n<p>If you’re just beginning your video marketing journey, Harp has several <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuam90Zm9ybS5jb20vYmxvZy92aWRlby1tYXJrZXRpbmctdGlwcy8%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">video marketing tips</a> you can use to start off right:</p> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><p>Each video should have a clear purpose</p><p></p></li> \n <p>To maintain clarity, always ask these three questions before making a video:</p> \n <ul> \n  <li><strong>Who is your target audience?</strong> Pinpoint your audience for each particular video. Be as specific as possible. For example, if you’re selling a diet plan, are you speaking to people with a particular health concern — losing weight, building muscles, developing six-pack abs, etc.? Knowing your audience makes it easier to both speak to them <em>and</em> measure the effectiveness of your video.</li> \n  <li><strong>What do you want them to feel?</strong> Stats are nice, but people likely won’t remember them. They will, however, remember how your video made them feel. Maybe you want them to feel hopeful, peaceful, energized, etc. This will spur them to the next part.</li> \n  <li><strong>What do you want them to do?</strong> Give them something to do, a next step. Make it as easy as possible. For example, have them call a number or visit a website — be sure to provide a URL to a page that talks specifically about what you covered in the video to maximize effectiveness. Get them in the pipeline and start them on the journey of becoming a customer.</li> \n </ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><p>Understand the importance of quality</p></li> \n <p>“Many people don’t know this, but audio quality is actually more important than video quality,” Harp advises. People will endure bad visual quality over bad audio quality. If they can’t hear what’s being said, they lose patience quickly. But if a video has good audio and not-so-great visuals, people tend to be more willing to stay in hopes that the video will improve.</p> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><p>Be consistent</p></li> \n <p>Make sure the videos you’re producing are consistent compared to one another and with your overall brand. For example, try to use the same intro for each video — the sound and style of graphics should be the same.</p> \n <p>“This lends itself to the <em>know, like, and trust</em> factors of sales,” Harp says. “For example, consider how GEICO and Progressive insurance have used the same spokespersons for their companies for years. They often even use the same colors, sounds, props, wardrobe, and set for their videos.”</p> \n</ol> \n<p>Now that you understand video marketing as a concept, let’s get into the benefits you can expect to receive from it.</p> \n<h2>Video marketing benefits, ROI, and social media</h2> \n<p>For years marketers have been shouting, “Content is king!”</p> \n<p>Why?</p> \n<p>Because content has helped many companies bring in more business. And given the rise in video consumption in recent years — <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9iaXRlYWJsZS5jb20vYmxvZy90aXBzL3ZpZGVvLW1hcmtldGluZy1zdGF0aXN0aWNzLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">55 percent of people view online videos every day</a> — video might be the front-runner for favorite type of content.</p> \n<p>There are plenty more stats where that came from, but in this chapter we’re looking at the reason those stats exist. So if you’re still on the fence about video marketing, the points below will ensure you’re aware of its upsides.</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"> \n  <img src=\"https://www.jotform.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Benefits-of-video-marketing-04-700x544.png\" alt=\"Video marketing benefits, ROI, and social media\" class=\"wp-image-295097\" /> \n </figure> \n</div> \n<h3>The importance of video marketing</h3> \n<p>“Video marketing gives you the opportunity to provide valuable information to businesses you want to work with,” says Ken Kerry, executive creative director at <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cDovL3d3dy5zY3JpcHR0b3NjcmVlbi5jb20v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">Script to Screen</a>. This information may be answers to specific questions your target audience has, advice about unique challenges they’re facing, or even clarifications regarding myths that could be holding potential customers back from making decisions.</p> \n<p>Kerry’s own video content marketing serves as a first impression of Script to Screen for a company that might be considering their services. His strategy is to provide content that not only shows his company’s capabilities (such as with an awareness video), but his team’s ability to address challenges or needs similar to the prospect’s (such as with a case study video).</p> \n<p>“Our belief is that, by presenting our expertise with tangible business results first, we create the ability and the permission to explore how we can best serve new clients,” Kerry says.</p> \n<h3>Benefits of video marketing</h3> \n<p>Aaron Nix,<a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cDovL3d3dy5hYXJvbm5peC5jb20v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\"> </a>assistant professor of art, video producer, and <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cDovL3d3dy5hYXJvbm5peC5jb20v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">filmmaker</a>, has helped conceptualize and create many videos. He calls out several key benefits of video marketing:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Improved engagement.</strong> Video gives you the ability to engage your target audience using more than just words. Higher engagement translates to more people watching more of your video, extending their interaction with your brand. “With video, your audience is more involved. Instead of just reading or quickly scrolling past an image, you capture their attention and engage their senses for an extended period of time,” he explains.</li> \n <li><strong>Increased brand awareness.</strong> “People are always looking to engage with other people’s stories and events. It’s a part of our social culture now,” he says. Since video is easily accessible in our media-saturated culture — live events, streaming, social media, etc. — people expect video and are drawn to it. While they may scroll past an image, video makes them pause. Using video gives you the opportunity to share your brand with more people, instead of being ignored.</li> \n <li><strong>More compelling storytelling.</strong> “The more senses you can engage, the more interesting you can make the story,” Nix explains. Video is much more dynamic than text or still images, which means you can communicate complex subject matter in a simpler way and convey important aspects like tone. People connect with stories, so creating a compelling one can help endear people to your brand.</li> \n <li><strong>Greater trust.</strong> “People are time-sensitive, so asking them to take even 30 seconds out of their day can be a big ask,” he says. If you’re able to give them something they like and engage with — whether it’s emotional, comedic, or something else — that builds trust with your brand.</li> \n</ul> \n<h3>Social media and video marketing</h3> \n<p>The average person spends <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuc3RhdGlzdGEuY29tL3N0YXRpc3RpY3MvNDMzODcxL2RhaWx5LXNvY2lhbC1tZWRpYS11c2FnZS13b3JsZHdpZGUv&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">144 minutes per day on social media</a> — nearly two and a half hours — and that number is trending upward every year. Is it any wonder that many experts recommend including social media as part of your video marketing efforts?</p> \n<p>“People’s eyes are constantly on their feeds, but there’s a massive amount of noise people have to wade through every day,” Nix explains. In addition, the digital intelligence of the average user has increased as people become more social media savvy. They expect more from video, so getting your target audience’s attention requires a well-produced, extremely relevant social media video they can connect with.</p> \n<h3>Achieving ROI with video marketing</h3> \n<p>Video ROI comes in many forms — it really depends on the type of business you operate. Nix shares a few example goals:</p> \n<ul> \n <li><strong>Recruiting people.</strong> Whether you’re looking to attract students, athletes, or employees, awareness is a big part of this goal, and it doesn’t always have clearly trackable metrics. Useful proxies are social media <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuam90Zm9ybS5jb20vYmxvZy92aWRlby1tZXRyaWNzLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">metrics</a>, such as a growing following. You can also use more direct means like sharing a video on social that links to a <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/what-is-a-landing-page.html\">landing page</a> and tracking performance. “Notably, video engagement is typically higher than any other post type on our social media pages,” says Nix of the college where he works.</li> \n <li><strong>Generating donations.</strong> Donations are a significant boon to nonprofits and colleges. A video/landing page combo comes in handy here, too, as you can share videos that speak to the causes donors care about. Nix says his college may share a video aimed at former students to elicit their support. “We typically have a specific campaign, such as for the annual day of giving, where we track performance for a specific class year to see how many responded versus donated.”</li> \n</ul> \n<p>Now you know how you can benefit from video marketing. Next, we walk through the main types of marketing videos you can make.</p> \n<h2>Types of videos</h2> \n<p>We’ve discussed a lot of concepts about video marketing, but now we move into the really interesting part — namely, the main types of videos you can create. Each has unique attributes you should be aware of to maximize their effectiveness.</p> \n<h3>6 video content types</h3> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Educational</h4></li> \n <p>Educational videos provide your audience — typically people who are already your customers — with information about your products, such as technical details or how best to use them in different situations. These types of videos are often used by software-as-a-service (SaaS) companies to instruct users how to navigate through the product to accomplish a specific goal.</p> \n <div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n  <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"> \n   <img src=\"https://www.jotform.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/Types-of-videos-700x544.png\" alt=\"education video marketing\" class=\"wp-image-295407\" /> \n  </figure> \n </div> \n <p>Lance Cummins, president of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9hbnl2b28uY29tLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">Anyvoo</a>, explains that such <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuam90Zm9ybS5jb20vYmxvZy9qb3Rmb3JtLTQtdmlkZW8tdHV0b3JpYWxzLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">tutorial videos</a> are most effective when they</p> \n <ul> \n  <li><strong>Sound conversational. </strong>People are fine being led, but they don’t necessarily want to be instructed. Tutorials should make users feel like someone is helping them accomplish something, not like they’re learning a lesson. “A conversational tone aids in making the experience real and genuine,” Cummins explains.</li> \n  <li><strong>Employ screen sharing. </strong>When you can hold a product in your hand, it’s a lot easier to reference specific parts of it in, say, an instructional manual. However, SaaS products tend to have lots of screens that look nearly identical to the average user, so it’s important that users be able to follow along — screen by screen — with a guide. Cummins points out that the mouse should be visible and screens should load in real time, as opposed to cutting these transitions. “You want the user to have a real experience — like they hopped on a screen share with someone from your company who’s walking them through the task.”</li> \n </ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Announcement</h4></li> \n <p>When your business has big news to share — for example, an upcoming merger or acquisition — this calls for an <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuam90Zm9ybS5jb20vYmxvZy81LW1pbGxpb24tdXNlcnMv&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">announcement video</a>. However, Cummins cautions against focusing on your business as part of the presentation. “I’m a big proponent of framing any announcement to focus on the person hearing the message — your prospects, customers, and so on.”</p> \n <p>When writing the script for your announcement, Cummins suggests that you ask yourself</p> \n <ul> \n  <li>What is this news going to do for my audience?</li> \n  <li>Why will they care?</li> \n  <li>How does this help them?</li> \n </ul> \n <p>“If you can’t answer these questions, then you should rethink doing the video in the first place,” Cummins says.</p> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Product launch</h4></li> \n <p><a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cueW91dHViZS5jb20vd2F0Y2g%2Fdj1sTGtlWjdraFN4dw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">Product launch videos</a> can be considered a type of announcement video since they announce when you’ve created or redesigned a new product, whether it’s tangible, such as a new car model, or intangible, like software. Whatever the case, your goal is to generate interest in your product. “You do this by helping your audience picture themselves using or experiencing what you’ve created,” Cummins says.</p> \n <p>He recommends producing a series of product launch videos, rather than just one. Multiple videos help people see a product from different perspectives, as well as consistently expose them to your product.&nbsp;</p> \n <p>“Avoid just listing out features you think they’ll like, for example, the fact that a new line of glasses is made from Titanium. Instead, focus on evoking emotions from your audience — for example, they may want to feel smart. Make a clear connection between those emotions and your product,” says Cummins.</p> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Company culture</h4></li> \n <p>Company culture videos are typically used to provide an inside look at your business — how the business works, what employees think about working there, etc. These videos can also be used to engage current employees at workplace events. “If you’re showcasing your company culture at an annual get-together, by all means brag on yourself and share inside jokes.”</p> \n <p>In contrast, Cummins notes you should take a different approach if your company culture video is meant to help recruit new employees: “As with announcement videos, your culture video should focus on how your company culture would benefit a newcomer in the organization. And be sure that, when people speak, they are conversational. You don’t want anyone to sound like they’re reading from a teleprompter — it comes off as stiff.”</p> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Q&amp;A</h4></li> \n <p>Q&amp;A videos give you the opportunity to address questions from users or prospects. For example, you may get a lot of questions from customers on ways your product can be used. You can quickly collect and keep track of these customer questions with <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuam90Zm9ybS5jb20v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">JotForm</a>, an easy-to-use form builder.</p> \n <p>Cummins recommends setting up Q&amp;A videos interview style, with one person asking questions and the other one answering. To make the video more dynamic, you can place text on either side of the scene.&nbsp;</p> \n <p>“This will help emphasize the question being asked,” Cummins says. “It will also help viewers who are watching the video for a specific question to easily find what they’re looking for.”</p> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Case study</h4></li> \n <p>Case study videos enable you to showcase how your organization has helped past clients overcome a particular challenge. For example, <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cueW91dHViZS5jb20vd2F0Y2g%2Fdj1UZkhzUHBkckNGayZhbXA7dD0zcw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">this case study video</a> walks through how one JotForm client uses the platform to make her <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/what-is-workflow.html\">workflow</a> easier — from collecting client consent forms to collecting client payments.</p> \n <p>“With case study videos, you definitely want the client to be a part of it,” Cummins advises, though that may mean you give up some degree of control. Still, the value in having a client speak to your organization’s capabilities will go a long way.</p> \n <p>In addition, case study videos can be a boon to video <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/email-marketing.html\">email marketing</a>. If you use email as a marketing tactic — cold <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/the-ultimate-cold-email-outreach-guide.html\">outreach</a>, automations, etc. — incorporating a case study video can help elicit a reply.</p> \n</ol> \n<p>With the different types of videos covered, we’ll discuss creating a video marketing strategy.</p> \n<h2>How to create a video marketing strategy</h2> \n<p>Developing a video marketing strategy isn’t too different from developing other marketing strategies, but the underlying medium naturally creates some distinctions — after all, video requires more time and money to produce than text or images. We discuss these distinctions below, along with steps you can take to develop a video marketing strategy of your own.</p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\"> \n <figure class=\"aligncenter size-large\"> \n  <img src=\"https://www.jotform.com/blog/wp-content/uploads/2020/03/video-marketing-strategy-06-700x544.png\" alt=\"steps you can take to develop a video marketing strategy\" class=\"wp-image-295267\" /> \n </figure> \n</div> \n<h3>5 steps to creating a video marketing strategy</h3> \n<ol> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Define your business objective</h4></li> \n <p>“When you first start thinking about video, stop thinking about video. Instead, think about what you’re doing as a business,” says Robert Weiss, president of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cDovL3d3dy5tdWx0aXZpc2lvbmRpZ2l0YWwuY29tLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">MultiVision Digital</a>. Are you launching a new product? Are you moving into a new line of business? Your video goals should support these initiatives.</p> \n <p>For example, you wouldn’t want to focus on corporate overview or culture videos if you’re announcing a new product — your spend should go to product launch videos. “Video works best when it’s integrated into a thoughtful plan. And that plan can certainly evolve over time as your objectives change,” notes Weiss.</p> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Understand your target audience</h4></li> \n <p>As with any marketing-focused effort, knowing who you’re speaking to is critical. You’ve no doubt already defined your target audience, but ensure you have an in-depth understanding of who they are and what they want.</p> \n <p>According to Weiss, knowing your audience inside and out is important for your production efforts and the costs associated with them. “It’s about added efficiency,” he says. “You can output multiple videos that speak to different audience segments while using the same basic video components. Just make a few changes and you have a whole new video — without scheduling a whole new shoot.”</p> \n <p>For example, consider an insurance company that wants to produce videos featuring experts talking about insurance. The information will be largely the same, but different customers look for specific insurance products or coverage.</p> \n <p>“The company can share the same insurance knowledge, but change up the talking points and visuals to focus on aspects that newlyweds or retirees care about most,” Weiss explains.</p> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Identify distribution channels</h4></li> \n <p>The <em>where</em> of your video marketing strategy is another important component. You have to decide how best to reach your target audience with your videos. “The exact mix of distribution will differ depending on your business and the types of videos you make,” explains Weiss.</p> \n <p>Here are a few channels you may decide to use:</p> \n <ul> \n  <li>Streaming platforms (Netflix, Hulu, etc.)</li> \n  <li>Social media (Facebook, Instagram, YouTube, etc.)</li> \n  <li>Google Ads networks</li> \n  <li>Your website</li> \n </ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Develop a video production budget</h4></li> \n <p>“I recommend starting small. You can test a monthly budget of around $1,000 until you’re satisfied with the results,” says Morten Storgaard, creator of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9wYXNzaXZlaW5jb21lZ2Vlay5jb20v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">PassiveIncomeGeek</a>. Then build up from there. A good video marketing budget is one that gives a promising return. As you add more to your budget and keep testing, you can further refine the idea of <em>good</em> and <em>acceptable</em> ROI.</p> \n <p>As far as what you’ll need to consider, Weiss calls out a few key elements:</p> \n <ul> \n  <li>Time and talent to write the script</li> \n  <li>Cameras and other equipment</li> \n  <li>Production and editing time</li> \n  <li>Motion graphics and color correction</li> \n  <li>Labor and experience of the crew</li> \n </ul> \n <li style=\"font-weight: 900;font-size: 18px;\"><h4 style=\"font-size: 18px;\">Create your videos</h4></li> \n <p>Video branding is essential to establishing yourself with your audience. Make sure to include elements like your logo, slogan, and brand colors within the first five to 10 seconds of each video, especially if the video is an ad.</p> \n <p>Remember that users can typically skip video ads after a few seconds, or scroll past them on social. “Unlike traditional video ads for TV and streaming platforms, you can’t afford to tell the story first and then expect the viewer to watch to the end to find out who you are,” Storgaard explains.</p> \n <p>Also consider <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/why-are-videos-essential-to-seo-in-2020-and-beyond.html\">video SEO</a> optimization to ensure your content is ranked and seen. Weiss says one video likely won’t cut it — you’ll need several, just like with blog posts in traditional content marketing. And speaking of content marketing, Weiss notes that adopting a video-first strategy can help achieve greater video optimization: “This strategy is about creating content for video, then turning that content into supporting blog posts, social media images, emails, and so on.”</p> \n</ol> \n<p>Creating your own video marketing strategy may seem like a big challenge, but the above guidance should give you a great foundation to start.</p> \n<h3>Meet your video marketing guides</h3> \n<h4>Aaron Nix</h4> \n<p>Aaron Nix currently serves as an assistant professor of art and video producer at Concordia University, Nebraska in Seward, where he leads courses in film production, film criticism, digital media, and photography. Through his <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cDovL3d3dy5hYXJvbm5peC5jb20v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">freelance work</a>, Nix has written and directed award-winning films and produced successful ad campaigns for clients nationwide.</p> \n<h4>Ken Kerry</h4> \n<p>Ken Kerry is the executive creative director at <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cDovL3d3dy5zY3JpcHR0b3NjcmVlbi5jb20v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">Script to Screen</a>. Ken cofounded the company in 1986, along with his wife, Barbara. Together, they built Script to Screen into one of the nation’s leading direct response television companies, producing more than 600 infomercials and DRTV spots, generating more than $6 billion in sales for clients and winning numerous awards for excellence.</p> \n<h4>Lance Cummins</h4> \n<p>Lance Cummins is the president of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9hbnl2b28uY29tLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">Anyvoo</a>, a scrappy maker-startup that helps remote workers revolutionize the way remote work is seen by handcrafting simple, professional video call backdrops. He’s also the president of Nectafy, a growth content agency that helps clients attract new business.</p> \n<h4>Morten Storgaard</h4> \n<p>Morten Storgaard is an online marketing veteran and creator of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9wYXNzaXZlaW5jb21lZ2Vlay5jb20v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\" target=\"_blank\" rel=\"noreferrer noopener\">PassiveIncomeGeek</a>. He has a background in e-commerce and has worked with large and small brands to establish awareness and drive sales online.</p> \n<h4>Randall Harp</h4> \n<p>Randall Harp is the creator in chief at <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9jaGFwZWxoaWxsbWVkaWEuY29tLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">Chapel Hill Media</a>. He has a diverse background in fine arts, film scoring, and software development for a variety of industries. With his experience, Harp creatively tells the stories of businesses through video — driving the production of strategic video assets, including scripts, storyboards, voice-overs, music, and motion graphics.</p> \n<h4>Robert Weiss</h4> \n<p>Robert Weiss is the president of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cDovL3d3dy5tdWx0aXZpc2lvbmRpZ2l0YWwuY29tLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113318\">MultiVision Digital</a>, a video content marketing company. He got started in video production and marketing nearly a decade ago and has produced over 800 videos addressing a wide array of business objectives.</p> \n<img
