23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"School Website Best Practices: Designing for Success","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113358","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"690\" height=\"435\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Feature.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">As students head into the fall semester, every school needs to have a solid tech strategy in place, and this all starts with a well-designed website.</p> \n<p>This rings especially true since many schools are trying to connect with large volumes of students and keep them updated throughout COVID-19 challenges.</p> \n<p>Having a well-designed education website is an ideal way to establish your digital presence, regardless if you work at a school with an existing web presence or are <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2Rlc2lnbi9idWlsZC15b3VyLWZpcnN0LXdlYnNpdGUtZnJvbS1zY3JhdGNoLmh0bWw%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">building your brand from the ground up</a>. Whether you’re aiming to impart knowledge or simply inform students about upcoming events, your website should provide your community with any information they’re seeking.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The best education websites support your goals by incorporating solid design principles. To help, we’ll walk through these three design elements that can make your school stand out to students and families:</p> \n<ol>\n <li>Develop engaging learning opportunities.</li>\n <li>Create a well-organized navigation bar.</li>\n <li>Offer straightforward forms.</li>\n</ol> \n<p>To easily incorporate these strategies, you’ll first need an intuitive content management system (CMS) built specifically for the education sector. These will offer education-based functionality that more generic ones won’t include. To kick off your search, take a look at <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9tb3J3ZWIub3JnL1Bvc3Qvc2Nob29sLXdlYnNpdGUtYnVpbGRlcnM%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">Morweb’s list of top school website builders</a>. This will help you choose one that supports your goals, which is vital to school web design success.</p> \n<p>Ready to create a beautiful school website that fully engages your students, prospects, parents, and faculty? Let’s jump in.&nbsp;</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Header-1.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113359\" />\n</figure> \n<h2>1. Develop engaging learning opportunities.</h2> \n<p>For the past several years, <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2luc3BpcmF0aW9uL3R1dG9yaWFscy1pbnNwaXJhdGlvbi90ZWNobm9sb2d5LWluLXRoZS1jbGFzc3Jvb20uaHRtbA%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">the growing prevalence of technology in the classroom</a> has been a major consideration for schools. Now, due to the pandemic, schools and educators are having to reevaluate how they communicate with students, hold classes remotely, and keep students engaged while at home. With many schools making the shift to remote learning, educators are scrambling to figure out how to provide an engaging learning experience online.</p> \n<p>Through your school’s website, you can provide valuable learning opportunities and stay connected with students at a safe social distance. Let’s explore three primary learning opportunities you can offer through your school website:</p> \n<ol>\n <li><strong>Offer eCourses. </strong>With the shift to virtual learning, <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9hcnRpc2FuZWxlYXJuaW5nLmNvbS9jdXN0b20tZGV2ZWxvcG1lbnQ%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">eCourses</a> allow teachers to continue sharing knowledge with students from a safe distance. Upload these lessons directly to your school’s website. With a website builder that offers a student portal, you can ensure only designated individuals access these courses.</li>\n <li><strong>Create online assignments.</strong> Quizzes and assignments are an essential part of the learning process. Especially as schools shift away from paper assessments, it’s important to incorporate e-learning tools into your curriculum. Using <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuam90Zm9ybS5jb20vZm9ybS10ZW1wbGF0ZXMvY2F0ZWdvcnkvcXVpei10ZW1wbGF0ZQ%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">an online form builder with templates</a>, your teachers will be able to quickly create these quizzes, which will then be automatically graded as students complete them. </li>\n <li><strong>Run a blog.</strong> Blogging enables you to share news and updates with your website visitors. While your marketing team will primarily run the blog, you may also consider allowing your students and faculty members to take charge and craft some of the posts themselves. Work with your team to determine which approach your school will take in advance.</li>\n</ol> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_news-blog.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113360\" />\n</figure> \n<p>Going virtual doesn’t mean you have to sacrifice quality. In fact, it gives your educators the opportunity to completely rethink the learning experience for students. Encourage your faculty to keep the above in mind when developing assignments and other educational content. Explore the concept of shifting to online learning further with <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2luc3BpcmF0aW9uL3R1dG9yaWFscy1pbnNwaXJhdGlvbi9lZHVjYXRpb25hbC10ZWNobm9sb2d5Lmh0bWw%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">this educational technology guide</a> to make the most of virtual classrooms.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Header-2.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113361\" />\n</figure> \n<h2>2. Create a well-organized navigation bar.</h2> \n<p>When you’ve taken the time to develop engaging content, you’ll want to ensure that your website visitors can find it. By developing a clear navigation bar, your audience will be able to locate whatever information is most relevant to their immediate needs. On the other hand, if they <em>can’t</em> find the desired information within a reasonable amount of time, they may become frustrated and leave your school’s website altogether.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_navigation-menu.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113362\" />\n</figure> \n<p>Consider your target audience. This likely includes your prospective students, your current students and staff members, and your alumni. When visiting your school’s website, these three groups have different intentions behind why they’re there. Because of this, it’s important to create the correct framework to help them find what they’re looking for. Let’s take a look at these three perspectives:</p> \n<ol>\n <li><strong>Prospective students:</strong> These individuals want to start with an overview of your school. This includes information such as its location and offered courses. From here, they may dive deeper to learn more about available programs and extracurricular activities. Otherwise, they may continue their search for education elsewhere.</li>\n <li><strong>Current students and staff members:</strong> This group is already familiar with your school, so you’ll need to take a slightly different approach for their experience with your navigation. These visitors will likely want to learn more about ongoing events (whether in-person or virtual), access a community program, or log into your student and faculty portal. This way, they can maximize their learning experience.</li>\n <li><strong>Alumni:</strong> For high schools and higher education institutions, individuals who have already graduated have a different set of needs altogether. They return to your school’s website looking to stay updated on any progress, engage in career networking opportunities, and possibly donate to their alma mater. Help them accomplish these goals by creating dedicated alumni pages, clear fundraising appeals, and accessible donation forms.</li>\n</ol> \n<p>From here, you’ll want to determine which information is most pertinent to each of these audiences, which will be used to form the information architecture within your navigation bar. Don’t include everything in your navigation bar, though. Instead, only feature your high-value pages, such as those discussed above.</p> \n<p>Often, you’ll see schools include button CTAs such as ‘Donate’ and ‘Enroll’ in the navigation bar as well. According to <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuc29hcGJveGVuZ2FnZS5jb20vYmxvZy8xODkxLWRvbmF0ZS1idXR0b24%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">Soapbox Engage’s donate button guide</a>, each button’s design can play an important role in generating conversions, so take the necessary time to create a straightforward design that stands out. If your CMS offers it, you can include a search bar to help visitors navigate to your other content.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Overall, remember that your navigation bar will be visible across your entire website. Whether a visitor lands on your <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2Rlc2lnbi9ob21lcGFnZS1kZXNpZ24tcHJhY3RpY2VzLmh0bWw%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">homepage</a> or a blog post, they should be able to quickly locate whatever they need using your navigation bar, whether it’s your donation form or information about upcoming events.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Header-3.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113363\" />\n</figure> \n<h2>3. Offer straightforward forms.</h2> \n<p>Chances are, your school employs various types of forms, such as those for donations, health information, and applications. Thanks to <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9qb3Rmb3JtLmNvbQ%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">online form builders</a>, you can now make yours available online. By placing these valuable resources directly on your school’s website, visitors will find them much easier to locate and will be able to fill them out without making an extra trip to your school. Not to mention, you won’t have to worry about organizing this data on your own later on.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_donation-form.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113364\" />\n</figure> \n<p><strong>Forms that are difficult to locate and navigate will turn users away.</strong> Instead, make sure they’re user-friendly, so you can effectively drive people through the process. Keep these best practices in mind to <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2Rlc2lnbi81LXdlYi1kZXNpZ24tZWxlbWVudHMtdGhhdC1pbXByb3ZlLXVzZXItZXhwZXJpZW5jZS5odG1s&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">improve the user experience</a> and boost form conversions:</p> \n<ul>\n <li><strong>Determine what information you’d like to collect. </strong>When someone clicks through to one of your forms (whether they’re looking to enroll, register for an event, or donate), dozens of fields will seem overwhelming. Then, they may choose to leave before ever starting. Instead, limit the number of fields to the basics. <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubW9yd2ViLm9yZy9Qb3N0L2RvbmF0aW9uLXBhZ2UtZGVzaWduLXRpcHMtZXhhbXBsZXM%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">For your donation page design</a>, this means name, contact details, and payment information. Each additional field will give the visitor another chance to leave the process.</li>\n <li><strong>Make sure it’s mobile-responsive.</strong> In 2019, <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9xdW9yYWNyZWF0aXZlLmNvbS9hcnRpY2xlL21vYmlsZS1tYXJrZXRpbmctc3RhdGlzdGljcw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">80% of online users</a> used a mobile device to search the internet, making it an important consideration in your school’s web design strategy. When it comes to your forms, each element (e.g. fields, images, text) should automatically resize itself based on the user’s screen size. This will make it easier for users to fill out the fields and complete the form on mobile devices, which is important since your students are primarily younger and rely heavily on mobile devices.</li>\n <li><strong>Brand it to your school.</strong> Sticking to the same font as well as two or three colors will make sure your forms are consistent with the rest of your website. You’ll want to include your school’s logo as well. These subtle elements can make a big difference in reminding users of why they’re there. If your forms look drastically different from the rest of your website, visitors may think they’ve somehow ended up on an untrustworthy third-party site.</li>\n</ul> \n<p>Once you’ve created <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuam90Zm9ybS5jb20vZm9ybS1kZXNpZ24v&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">well-designed forms</a>, you’ll want to ensure they’re visible across your school’s website. As we mentioned earlier, your high-value forms should be featured in your navigation bar for quick access. From health forms to event registrations, ensure your communications team spends sufficient time designing these to drive conversions.</p> \n<h3>The Gist</h3> \n<p>Making <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubm91cGUuY29tL2RldmVsb3BtZW50L25vbnByb2ZpdC13ZWItZGV2ZWxvcG1lbnQuaHRtbA%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">smart design choices</a> can boost your brand and elevate your appeal to students, families, and faculty. A well-designed school website is a vital component of any education venture, regardless of your goals.</p> \n<p>While there’s much more that goes into effective school web design, these three design elements will serve as a great starting point. Regardless of the criteria you set in place for what an “award-winning” school web design looks like, it’s important that it be clear, navigable, and accessible. <strong>How does your school’s current website stack up?</strong><br />To position your school for success, check out <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9tb3J3ZWIub3JnL1Bvc3QvYmVzdC1zY2hvb2wtd2Vic2l0ZXM%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113358\">this list</a> of best school website designs. It provides examples of exceptional school websites so you can draw inspiration. Best of luck!</p> \n<img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113358\" width=\"1\" height=\"1\" style=\"display: none;\" />","descriptionType":"html","publishedDate":"Fri, 21 Aug 2020 +0000","feedId":2999,"bgimg":"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Feature.jpg","linkMd5":"6dbbe82f646adb25eee3f780b8e89791","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn77@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-38-704_84bc1a0dcc998b1d.webp","destWidth":690,"destHeight":435,"sourceBytes":83979,"destBytes":31376,"author":"Murad Bushnaq","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Feature.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn77@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-38-704_84bc1a0dcc998b1d.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Header-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx1/cdn89@2020_1/2020/08/24/15-51-45-326_574e72eb8cb3b64a.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_news-blog.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx23/cdn5@2020_6/2020/08/24/15-51-44-111_39d7aad0e32e7232.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Header-2.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx24/cdn62@2020_3/2020/08/24/15-51-44-411_e3919d2234ae8795.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_navigation-menu.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn25@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-47-336_281fb5e1e5bf7428.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_Header-3.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn77@2020_3/2020/08/24/15-51-45-038_3c2215f3bf57bf7f.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Morweb_Noupe_School-Website-Best-Practices-Designing-for-Success_donation-form.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx2/cdn94@2020_6/2020/08/24/15-51-42-109_0557b2f39c08ceb3.webp","https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113358":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx12/cdn9@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-40-661_223588f5218f292a.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598284297205},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"Japanese Minimalism in UI Design for Digital Products","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113116","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"1000\" height=\"471\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Untitled-1-1.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">In this article, I’m considering the concept of Japanese minimalism, its implications in the <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/design/what-makes-a-good-user-interface.html\">user interface</a> design of digital products, and its key principles.</p> \n<p>Are you ready to immerse in Japanese art trends leveraged in the context of the modern digital world?</p> \n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\">\n <p><em>“Be content with what you have; rejoice in the way things are. When you realize there is nothing lacking, the whole world belongs to you.” — Lao Tzu</em></p>\n</blockquote> \n<p>Konnichiwa, and welcome to the overview of the digital product design trend emphasizing the beauty of Japanese minimalism in the modern digital world. Here old art traditions combine with digital technologies, and the ancient stays side by side with innovation. This incredible cohesion of styles and technologies has given birth to a new trend in product user interface design — Japanese neo-minimalism. Let’s dive deeper into the history of the concept and see incredible samples of this style implemented in UI design for mobile apps and websites.</p> \n<h2>Minimalism Deep-Rooted in Japanese Art</h2> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/2-1024x769.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113117\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Illustration by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvOTM1OTczMy1Ja2lnYWk%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Ani Chitishvili</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<p>When thinking of minimalism, Japanese interior and graphic design are likely the first things coming to mind. Japanese minimalism takes roots in traditional Zen Buddhism aesthetics, the minimalist movement that carries the mission of keeping life simple and uncluttered by focusing on the bare essentials.</p> \n<p>At the heart of it is MA (lit., “gap”, “space”, “pause”), a Japanese cultural concept meaning the love to not things but space between them. It is all about the negative space, emptiness, and clearness. MA is usually considered as space where the absence of things means more than the presence of them. It is filled with nothing but energy and feeling. Ma means silence as opposed to sound and lack as opposed to excess.</p> \n<p>This concept moves us away from modern consumerism and helps re-connect with simplicity, naturalness, and functionality. It’s relished in interior design, architecture, art, music, and other Japanese life aspects. It has also become one of the most significant sources of inspiration for digital product creators worldwide. Today, you can see many examples of <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9maXJlYXJ0LnN0dWRpby9ibG9nLzUtcmVhc29ucy10by1hcHBseS1kaWdpdGFsLWlsbHVzdHJhdGlvbi1pbi13ZWItZGVzaWduLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">digital illustrations in web design</a> featuring Japanese minimalist aesthetics.</p> \n<h2>Principles of Japanese Minimalist Aesthetics in UI Design</h2> \n<p>Let’s think of Google. The world’s top brand has implemented all principles of Japanese minimalism in its memorable yet straightforward design. It is full of emptiness and meaning at the same time. It is clear and simple. It celebrates the beauty of contrast and bold typography. And it keeps a focus on the most important.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/3.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113118\" />\n</figure> \n<h3>The Use of Negative Space</h3> \n<p>In this case, negative is positive. The negative space (or white space) is the emptiness between elements in the user interface design. Modern brands leverage the power of negative space in web design and mobile app design to emphasize the importance of existing things. Using negative spaces helps avoid cognitive user overload and keep design intuitive.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The white space is a friend of user-friendliness in UI design for digital products. It allows emphasizing the most important and focusing attention on the essential content. By removing all the necessary things, we remain the most important and help the user easily find it in an interface. The most successful products are mostly easy-to-use, minimalist, and have a lot of negative space in the UI.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113119\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>UI App Animation by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvMTI2OTY4MDEt&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Movica</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5-1024x768.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113120\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>The concept for Sushi Delivery by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvMTM5OTEzMDctQ29uY2VwdC1mb3Itc3VzaGktZGVsaXZlcnk%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Yevhenia Tsmokalenko</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<h3>Simplicity &amp; Clearness</h3> \n<blockquote class=\"wp-block-quote\">\n <p><em>“Simple can be harder than complex: You have to work hard to get your thinking clean to make it simple. But it’s worth it in the end because once you get there, you can move mountains.” — Steve Jobs</em></p>\n</blockquote> \n<p>Simplicity is not only about how it looks but also how it functions. Let’s consider simplicity from the UX perspective. A simple user interface design empowers users to navigate between the web pages or app screens easily. It makes them enjoy interacting with the UI and gives them confidence that they can quickly accomplish tasks and goals they’re using your digital product for.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Japanese minimalism implies the absence of the cluttering details and decorations but keeping everything simple, elegant, strict, and clear. An excellent example of this is a mobile app design below.&nbsp;</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/6.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113121\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Uniqlo E-Commerce App Animation by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvNDM2NjA3My1VbmlxbG8tRS1Db21tZXJjZS1BcHAtQW5pbWF0aW9u&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Michal Skvarenina</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<h3>Contrast</h3> \n<p>Japanese minimalism is in love with the art of contrasts. Traditionally, it uses red &amp; white and white &amp; black combinations the most often. The frequent color combination is also red-blue-white. The monochromatic and high-contrast palette reveals the elegance of a digital product and gives it a fresh and modern look.</p> \n<p>Furthermore, high-contrast design increases the content readability and enables users to consume information more easily. The UI clarity, understandability, and ease of use are key goals of intelligent UX design, and a contrast color palette may help achieve them faster. The two examples below show how you can apply it to mobile app design.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/7-1024x768.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113122\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Self-Motivation App by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vRmlyZWFydC1k&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Fireart Studio</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/8.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113123\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Design by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvNTU4Nzk5MS1UZWEtQnJlYWs%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Mathilde Glib</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<h3>Dramatic Typography</h3> \n<p>We often associate the Japanese culture with Kanji, the adopted logographic Chinese characters used in the Japanese writing system. Inspired by Kanji’s distinguishable beauty, digital designers often create typography of a similar mood and look.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Japanese minimalism tends to use bold typography, and we can see the same tendency in the UI design of many new digital products. Large Japanese typography implemented in high-contrast palette creates a feeling of drama and intrigue. It helps shape an unforgettable online brand image and lasting impression from a website or mobile application. Are you looking to build a memorable brand for your digital product? Just try adding a bit of dramatism to its design by leveraging high-contrast color and bold typography, like Japanese art senseis have done it for their masterpieces.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113124\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Logo by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvNTg2OTIzOS05MC0xMDAtRGFpbHktU21hcnQtTG9nby1DaGFsbGVuZ2U%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Insigniada&nbsp;</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113125\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>UI Web Design by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vZHJld3Jpb3M%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Drew Rios</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/11.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113126\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Web Design for the Japanese Restaurant by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvMTIyMDUyMTUtSmFwYW5lc2UtUmVzdGF1cmFudA%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Sofia Pham</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<h3>The Focus on Essentials</h3> \n<p>Japanese people are thought to be masters of concentration since all the local religious and philosophical movements say about the importance of this human ability. Are they? Probably, we’ll never know until visit Japan in reality. However, local art brightly demonstrates it.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Japanese design is usually ultra-minimalist and focuses the viewer’s attention on one or several elements located in the center. There are no distracting details and unnecessary decorations in the user interface. This design is most often concentrated on the functionality first, and the visual part after. Mobile app designs presented below are great examples of this peculirity.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/12.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113127\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Signup Screen by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvNDUxNDM1NC1TaWduLXVw&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Oleg Frolov</em></a>\n  <br />\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/13.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113128\" />\n <figcaption>\n  <em>Sakana App by </em>\n  <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9kcmliYmJsZS5jb20vc2hvdHMvNjE5NjI3Mi1TYWthbmEtQXBwLUN1c3RvbS1UcmFuc2l0aW9ucw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113116\"><em>Yury Kirsanov</em></a>\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<h2>Less is More Today</h2> \n<p>Less is more. “More” may feel too cluttering and obtrusive for the user’s overloaded mind in the noisy modern world. Minimalism remains the optimal option for digital products. Rooting in Japanese culture and widely spread around the globe, the art of minimalism has conquered the hearts of millions of people today. It has become a continuous trend bringing a fresh look and ease of use to digital products. I hope that this article will help you reinforce your inner creative engine and inspire you to produce even more amazing minimalist designs for your next projects.<br /></p> \n<img +0000","feedId":2999,"bgimg":"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Untitled-1-1.jpg","linkMd5":"6e8cc0db6bd98ad12c641342548403ee","bgimgJsdelivr":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn9@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-38-079_d8dc462df098bc7d.webp","destWidth":1000,"destHeight":471,"sourceBytes":38215,"destBytes":8216,"author":"Dana Kachan","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Untitled-1-1.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn9@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-38-079_d8dc462df098bc7d.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/2-1024x769.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn93@2020_1/2020/08/24/15-51-40-409_e6b3f4fbea0c0d6f.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/3.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn45@2020_1/2020/08/24/15-51-47-672_79499f3c2458843f.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/4.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx30/cdn73@2020_3/2020/08/24/15-51-47-763_6e4a434f67563000.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/5-1024x768.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn98@2020_3/2020/08/24/15-51-47-259_20f6b4c05f611392.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/6.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn57@2020_6/2020/08/24/15-52-05-826_cda7e0724fde94b0.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/7-1024x768.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn98@2020_2/2020/08/24/15-51-43-716_84f9aa1116ac8624.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/8.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx/cdn50@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-40-815_5e5a5785392a444f.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/9.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn29@2020_2/2020/08/24/15-51-40-280_7a8c4d6c8922dd3b.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/10.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx15/cdn34@2020_3/2020/08/24/15-51-44-710_933c853a3de9e4f5.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/11.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn86@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-42-129_a89f362166ecb2a8.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/12.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx13/cdn73@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-45-515_53daa8de9b419780.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/13.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn57@2020_1/2020/08/24/15-51-46-948_1589c240380419d0.webp","https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113116":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx19/cdn5@2020_6/2020/08/24/15-51-41-667_3bcb6dd169df5180.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598284297220},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"8 Project Management Tips for Your Next Web Development Project","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113324","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"1024\" height=\"683\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/alvaro-reyes-qWwpHwip31M-unsplash-1024x683.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">Here’s the thing: No matter how great your web development idea is, you are likely to fail without the right management system.</p> \n<p>To become a successful web developer, you need to be effective in managing your web development projects. Doing so allows you to deliver a project on time.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>In case you are not aware, your revenues do not grow overnight. It would be best if you come up with the proper plan to execute your strategies.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Here are the eight project management tips that you can apply on your next web development project:</p> \n<h2>Create a detailed and actionable plan</h2> \n<p>The key to a successful project is breaking it up into smaller tasks.</p> \n<p>According to one episode of the <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cucHJvamVjdC1tYW5hZ2VtZW50LXBvZGNhc3QuY29tLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113324\">PM Podcast</a>, a project plan allows you to succeed. This is where Agile project management could come in handy.</p> \n<p>This project management approach provides you with a clear picture of what direction you are heading. It also gives you an insight into the impact of your actions, the risks involved, and how this will help you.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>It also has four primary components:</p> \n<ul>\n <li>Why or the Project Vision</li>\n <li>What or the Project Mission</li>\n <li>Who or your team members</li>\n <li>Success Criteria&nbsp;</li>\n</ul> \n<h2>Get to know your team</h2> \n<p>It is common to work with a team when doing a web development project. Your team is composed of developers and designers who you rely on to complete a project.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Your team will be the one who will take your project from start to finish.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Team members that work with one another are the most effective. So, you need to invest your time getting to know them. This includes understanding their workflows, personalities, usual schedule, and so on.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Doing so allows you to communicate effectively with them. And when it is easy for you to establish communication, you can plan and organize tasks, set milestones, and enjoy working with your team.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Organize a kickoff meeting</h2> \n<p>A meeting aims to create a foundation for your project. It’s also a fantastic opportunity for you to inspire and energize your team.</p> \n<p>The main goal of having a kickoff meeting is to align everyone in your team with your main project objectives. This is also a great time to discuss any misunderstandings or problems with your project.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>During the meeting, you should <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cud2ViZnguY29tL2Jsb2cvd2ViLWRlc2lnbi93ZWItZGV2ZWxvcG1lbnQta2lja29mZi1tZWV0aW5nLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113324\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">discuss your project’s primary purpose</a> with your team. This includes the essential success factors, goals, deliverables, start and end date, your project or communication plans, and so much more.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Invest in a reliable project management software</h2> \n<p>To make your project management tasks run smoothly, you should create a centralized source of information that your team can access anytime.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>This also makes communication with everyone in your team a lot easier.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>A great solution to this is to research a <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuYmVld2l0cy5jb20vd2ViLWRlc2lnbi1wcm9qZWN0LW1hbmFnZW1lbnQtc29mdHdhcmUv&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113324\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">great project management software</a>.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Project management software allows your team to stay connected as you work on a project. This helps avoid any unnecessary confusion and enables you to get things done a lot quicker.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Create a hub for organizing everything</h2> \n<p>If you’re working on a web development project, it is not surprising that you will need documentation. That’s because your documentation can only help you <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuc2l0ZXBvaW50LmNvbS9vcmdhbml6ZS1wcm9qZWN0LWZpbGVzLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113324\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">organize it well</a>, and it’s easy to locate.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>That’s why you need to use a tool that will allow sub-folders and let you house various assets, like Dropbox and Google Drive.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>You can visit this weekly to help you organize folders as you create new documentation, allowing any member of your team to navigate them with ease.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>If you’re using JIRA or Trello, use quick links on the documentation stored on this hub. You can also create a shared document with quick links that store things like designs, notes, and wireframes.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Doing so allows you to access the whole project easily. Remember, what’s crucial to the design team may not be as essential to the development team. Thus, you might need to create different versions of this project document.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Communicate with your team</h2> \n<p>It would help if you communicated your needs and expectations to your designers and developers. Although this might be challenging since project managers, <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/design/web-developer-portfolio-examples.html\">web developers</a>, and designers come from different spectrums.</p> \n<p>Project managers are often known to be the “idea people,” while developers and designers are more on the technical side.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>That’s why you need to focus on communicating the right idea and paint a clear picture of the type of software solution that you want developers and designers to build.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Come up with a risk management plan</h2> \n<p>Risks can hurt the success of your project. That’s why you need to know the risks that can come up early on.</p> \n<p>The key here is to anticipate the risks that can happen and how it can impact your web development project.</p> \n<p>High impact risks are usually the most severe. Meanwhile, low or unlikely chances can post the least threat.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>It would be ideal for creating a <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9ydWJ5Z2FyYWdlLm9yZy9ibG9nL3Jpc2stbWFuYWdlbWVudC1pbi1kZXZlbG9wbWVudA%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113324\">risk mitigation plan</a>. Doing so allows you to decrease the impact of a risk or prevent it from happening. You can start with the high impact risks and deal with the medium and low threats a little later.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>It also helps that you regularly review these risks, and then add new ones later.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Focus on one milestone at a time</h2> \n<p>While it can be easy to get ahead of yourself, especially if the project is successful in the early stages, this can be damaging in the long run.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Think about it- you can’t come up with seating for your restaurant if you don’t create a kitchen first. Similarly, you shouldn’t develop the frontend of your software if your backend is missing.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The key here is to achieve one milestone at a time. Slow and steady wins the race. Start by making small goals while you stay focused on the bigger picture.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Remember that web projects are not easy. But it does not mean that they can’t be fun and rewarding. It may be daunting at first, but with the right strategies and tools, you will end up a winner in the long run.</p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<p><em>Photo by </em><a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly91bnNwbGFzaC5jb20vQGFsdmFyb3JkZXNpZ24%2FdXRtX3NvdXJjZT11bnNwbGFzaCZhbXA7dXRtX21lZGl1bT1yZWZlcnJhbCZhbXA7dXRtX2NvbnRlbnQ9Y3JlZGl0Q29weVRleHQ%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113324\"><em>Alvaro src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/BvgAmfNCEAE0F8B.jpeg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"eye drawing with tears\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">For artists who are just beginning to draw people portraits, it may seem quite intimidating.</p> \n<p>In principle, the time you spend on drawings of people is directly parallel to the degree of life-likeness of your creation. As you devote more hours to a drawing you can naturally dive deeper into details and use your brush or pencil in a more cautious manner. </p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/minutes-1.jpg\" alt=\"eye drawing\" class=\"wp-image-113349\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Just like anything that needs some experience, mastering drawings of people takes time and only gets better when you practice enough in the long run. Refining your craft is not limited to the amount of practice only, there are some tips and tricks that will help you get there faster.&nbsp;&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Don’t forget that there are countless different ways to draw people, so it is important to develop your own by combining these best practices.</p> \n<h3><strong>Study face proportions carefully</strong></h3> \n<p>Face proportions can make or break your drawing. This fundamentally important factor is quite hard to achieve. However, it is the structure of your drawing so you have to get it right.<br /><br />A face that is oddly proportioned will look wrong and disturb anyone who looks at it. That is why you have to pay close attention to the distance between eyes, ears, nose, and mouth and their general ratio on the face in order to please the eyes. </p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/proportions.jpg\" alt=\"facial proportions\" class=\"wp-image-113354\" />\n</figure> \n<h3><strong>Understanding the bone structure&nbsp;</strong></h3> \n<p>Scaling<strong> </strong>the ratio of facial bones, the length of the chin, forehead, and the width of the face, cheekbone alignment is also difficult to get it straight. When you are drawing a face from scratch, careful examination of the relationship between key facial features will lead to more realistic drawings.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image is-resized\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/bone.jpg\" alt=\"drawings of different kinds of noses\" class=\"wp-image-113340\" width=\"572\" height=\"786\" />\n <figcaption>\n  by Giovanni Civardi\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<p>Focusing on one feature at a time will help you read the facial anatomy more carefully. After you dig out which details to look for you will intuitively know how to capture these lines in your drawing.</p> \n<h3><strong>Use shadows for maximum impact </strong></h3> \n<p>Getting the face proportions and bone structure right is important. However, it is not enough to make your artwork look three dimensional and realistic. That’s when the shadows come into the light. Talk about a bad pun! Joking aside, shadows and shades will save your drawing from looking just flat.&nbsp; </p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter is-resized\">\n  <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/img_5596.jpg\" alt=\"process of shading an eye drawing\" class=\"wp-image-113339\" width=\"562\" height=\"764\" />\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>First, you need to understand how lighting works in order to reach the ultimate level of mastering drawings of people. Creating the illusion of flow by skillfully acquiring basic lighting and shading techniques will help you discern the primary characteristics of the natural human form.</p> \n<h3><strong>The bigger, the better</strong></h3> \n<p>When you look at realistic drawings of people, you will realize that usually using paper or a canvas of a bigger dimension results in hyper-realistic artworks.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image is-resized\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/arms.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113351\" width=\"594\" height=\"702\" />\n</figure> \n<p>You can fit a head both into a letter-sized paper or an A1 paper. However, the amount of details that you can include while drawing on a smaller canvas is limited.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image is-resized\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/eyebrows.jpg\" alt=\"drawings of eyes\" class=\"wp-image-113346\" width=\"592\" height=\"1051\" />\n <figcaption>\n  by Nadia Coolrista\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<p>On a smaller paper, you cannot draw skin pores, or let’s say 150 eyebrow hair in a way that turns your creation into a realistically rendered one. This doesn’t mean that a smaller drawing is not a success however it certainly limits your capacity and talent.</p> \n<h4>Now it’s time to take a look at some successful examples of drawings of people to better understand which areas to focus on:</h4> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image is-resized\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/drawing.jpg\" alt=\"eye drawing\" </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image is-resized\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/male-face.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113353\" width=\"586\" height=\"733\" />\n <figcaption>\n  by Ani Cinski\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image is-resized\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/NIL-Tech.jpg\" alt=\"girl drawing 2\" class=\"wp-image-113337\" width=\"590\" height=\"743\" />\n</figure> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image is-resized\">\n <img  by Gabriel Vinicius\n  </figcaption>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<p>Knowing the human body and face is the key to master drawings of people. Remember the first sketch of your drawing will always be the hardest but practice will gradually improve your skills.</p> \n<p>Applying manageable techniques while maintaining your own style will help you refine your drawings in no time. 24/15-51-40-245_98e80e922c61062f.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/old-man.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx8/cdn62@2020_6/2020/08/24/15-51-40-799_463efb62fb04bbc2.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/8eef6653f319edf2f7ffd3b9d44d596e.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx11/cdn81@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-43-949_5f70b63ea015be63.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/0fe58c3b34c0a0734b64fedec7019c19.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx21/cdn21@2020_6/2020/08/24/15-51-40-839_a45f46f7dcd79ce3.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Screen-Shot-2020-08-21-at-15.17.10-953x1024.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx16/cdn29@2020_3/2020/08/24/15-51-42-800_ab43566d844557fb.webp","https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113332":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx29/cdn89@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-40-778_0736a9b198f24700.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598284297206},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">Getting inked has become a lot more popular recently, but tattoos are not something recent. In fact, tattoos are deeply embedded in human history and play an important role in many cultures and traditions.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>The oldest evidence that tattooing existed comes from the Upper Paleolithic period in Europe, where there are tools that signal people got inked 40,000 years ago. The earliest solid proof is found on Otzi the Iceman, who lived somewhere between 3300-3100 BC.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>So, in this article, we wanted to go over some of the traditional tattoo styles that still endure to this day. We’ve searched far and wide to find the best examples of each. It’s important to remember that, when people refer to traditional tattoos, they are usually talking about traditional American tattoos, but we thought that it wouldn’t do justice to other traditional tattoo styles.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>So in this article, we’ll be going over Japanese tattoos, Nordic tattoos, Polynesian tattoos, and traditional American tattoos.&nbsp; So, without too much delay, let’s get right into it.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2><strong>American Traditional Tattoos</strong></h2> \n<p>While we’re not a huge fan of traditional American tattoos, their popularity cannot be denied. Traditional American tattoos are defined by their symbolism and bright colors. </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<h2>Traditional Japanese Tattoos</h2> \n<p>Did you know that tattooing is illegal in Japan? Inking has been outlawed for the last 200 years but still, people carry the vibrant and iconic Japanese style tattoos all over their bodies proudly. Tattooing in Japan has been carried mostly by underground artists, or a rare few who had a medical license to do so. Traditional Japanese tattoos include cultural symbols, a vibrant color palette, and are usually large tattoos that can cover an entire limb or even the whole body. Most iconic designs usually include the Koi fish, dragons, tigers, oni (Japanese devils), and Lotus themed designs. </p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img </figcaption>\n </figure>\n</div> \n<h2>Traditional Polynesian Tattoos</h2> \n<p>Polynesia refers to the islands and tribes that are a part of Oceania. The Polynesian triangle is the home of many island tribes such as the Samoans, Hawaiians, the Maori, Tahitians, Cook Islanders, Marquesans, and Tongans. While there are slight cultural variations between tribes such as some variances in languages, inking remains a central and irreplaceable aspect of all Polynesian cultures. In fact, it was so important that tribe members who shied away from getting inked were shunned from the community and people who had incomplete tattoos would carry them as a reminder of their weakness for the rest of their lives. Traditional Polynesian tattoos are a bit different than the rest of the tattoo traditions on this article and don’t fall under tribal tattoos as their symbolism comes from patterns and the body parts they are inked on. A tattoo that is on the chest or arm means something entirely different than a tattoo on the lower body even if the designs might seem similar. </p> \n<div class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <figure class=\"aligncenter\">\n  <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/Samoan-tattoo.jpeg\" alt=\"traditional polynesian tattoo maori warrior tattoo\" class=\"wp-image-113243\" />\n </figcaption>\n</figure> \n<h2>Nordic Tattoos</h2> \n<p>While there are conflicting historical reports on wether Vikings were inked or not, Nordic styled tattoos are great both because of the patterns used and the symbolism behind them. The intricate nordic themed patterns woven together with mythological signs make up for great tattoos that both are good looking and hold meanings behind them. </p> \n<figure \n<p>All in all, we love tattoos, tattoos are cool. Carrying a great artists’ art on your body is a great honor. While tattoos are getting increasingly popular in the last few decades, they have their roots in the history of our kind and that makes them even cooler! If you think we did any injustice to any tattoo style or if you believe another type of traditional tattoo styles should be featured in this article, leave us a comment. If you know any great tattoos that would fit this article or if you have one yourself, reach out! ammer-Thor-Odin-Rune-Pagan-Norse-Asatru-Regular-Crew-T-Shirt-BL-Small-3X-Choice-of-Colors-FREE-US-Shipping-1.jpeg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx33/cdn26@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-41-694_525f8fdf903bc5a9.webp","https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113134":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx32/cdn41@2020_1/2020/08/24/15-51-41-276_e63f6e85cdea5fd4.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598284297229},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"A Handbook on “GO AGILE”!","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113299","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"1024\" height=\"681\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/glenn-carstens-peters-RLw-UC03Gwc-unsplash-1024x681.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">Agile is a procedure by which a team can deal with a project by separating it into a few stages and including steady coordinated effort with stakeholders and consistent improvement and emphasis at each phase of the task. It starts with clients laying out how the finished result will be utilized and what issue it will resolve.</p> \n<h2><strong>What is Scrum?</strong></h2> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image4.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113305\" />\n</figure> \n<ol>\n <li>Scrum is a subset of Agile. It is a lightweight process framework for agile development, and one of the most widely used one.</li>\n <li>It’s not a process or methodology.</li>\n <li>Easy to understand.</li>\n <li>Based on Empiricism which means that scrum artifacts should be transparent to everyone in the team.</li>\n</ol> \n<h2><strong>Principles of Agile</strong></h2> \n<ol>\n <li>To fulfil the client through right on time and continuous use of important software.</li>\n <li>To cater to changing requirements, even late in <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9lbnRlcnByaXNlLmFmZmxlLmNvbS9tb2JpbGUtYXBwLWRldmVsb3BtZW50&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113299\">app development</a>.</li>\n <li>Delivering working software frequently.</li>\n <li>Stakeholders work with the scrum team together throughout the project so as to avoid any communication gaps.</li>\n <li>The most efficient way of communicating information within the team is face-to-face conversation.</li>\n <li>The progress of work is measured by working software.</li>\n <li>Continuous attention is paid to technical excellence.</li>\n <li>Due to the self-organizational team structure, the best architectures, designs, and ideas come up.</li>\n</ol> \n<h2><strong>Empiricism</strong></h2> \n<ol>\n <li><strong>Transparency:-</strong> All artifacts of the process should be visible to the stakeholders and the scrum team. Due to transparency, they can inspect the current state of the project and take necessary action if needed.</li>\n <li><strong>Inspection:-</strong> Having regular inspections of artifacts will help the stakeholders to incorporate changes in order to achieve the goal.</li>\n <li><strong>Adaptation:-</strong> Improvements can be made by adjusting the process based on the inspection results.</li>\n</ol> \n<h2><strong>Scrum is Iterative and Incremental</strong></h2> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image5-2.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113300\" />\n</figure> \n<p><strong><em>First one – Incremental</em></strong><br /><strong><em>Second one – Iterative</em></strong></p> \n<p><strong>Incremental:-</strong> This type of development is to build small increments of the entire product. Each increment adds more features to the product. After multiple increments, you will get the complete product.</p> \n<p><strong>Iterative:- </strong>This development is to build something, take some <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/constructive-feedback.html\">feedback</a>, and then refining to make it better. This will keep happening until we receive the product of good quality.</p> \n<h2><strong>The Scrum Team:</strong></h2> \n<ol>\n <li>The Product Owner.</li>\n <li>The Development Team.</li>\n <li>The Scrum Master.</li>\n</ol> \n<h2><strong>The Product Owner</strong></h2> \n<p>The product owner is liable for augmenting the estimation of the product and work of the development group.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image1-3.png\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113301\" />\n</figure> \n<ol>\n <li>Clearly describing the Product backlog items.</li>\n <li>Responsible for managing the product backlog.</li>\n <li>To ensure the PBI is visible and clear to all.</li>\n <li>To ensure the requirement is understood by all to the level it is required.</li>\n <li>Accountable for building high-value products.</li>\n <li>Ordering of Product backlog items to achieve the best goals.</li>\n <li>Responsible for understanding and answering all questions pertaining to the product domain.</li>\n <li>Responsible for tracking the release progress.</li>\n <li>Liable for making and dealing with the release plans.</li>\n <li>Liable for making and building up the product vision.</li>\n <li>Enhancing the estimation of work done by the development team.</li>\n</ol> \n<h2><strong>The Development Team</strong></h2> \n<p>The Development Team comprises experts who accomplish crafted by conveying a conceivably releasable Increment of “Done” product at the end of each Sprint.</p> \n<ol>\n <li>Cross-functional and self-organizing.</li>\n <li>Participates in all scrum events.</li>\n <li>Responsible for creating the product increment.</li>\n <li>Collaborates with the Product Owner for optimal value.</li>\n <li>Responsible for identifying and eliminating technical debts.</li>\n <li>Liable for creating and coordinating the sprint backlog.</li>\n <li>Responsible for implementing good engineering practices.</li>\n <li>Helps product owners in backlog management by explaining the technical constraints.</li>\n <li>Answerable for learning all the functions required to convey a product increment.</li>\n <li>Answerable for following the advancement of the sprint.</li>\n</ol> \n<h2><strong>The Scrum Master:</strong></h2> \n<p>The scrum master is responsible for ensuring that Scrum is understood and enacted by all. He ensures that the scrum team adheres to Scrum practices and rules.</p> \n<ol>\n <li>He is a servant- leader to the scrum team.</li>\n <li>Responsible for building the product fast by eliminating impediments.</li>\n <li>Goes about as a change agent that builds the <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/inspiration/productivity-the-ultimate-guide.html\">productivity</a> of the scrum team.</li>\n <li>Mentors the development team for self-organization and cross-functionality.</li>\n <li>Helps the product owners prioritize the work and teaches stakeholders value-based prioritization.</li>\n <li>Facilitates Scrum events as requested or required.</li>\n <li>Finds and teaches techniques for effective product backlog management to the product owners.</li>\n <li>Enables workers and partners of the association to comprehend and institute Scrum and experimental product development.</li>\n <li>Assists with streamlining the outside connection with the scrum group to amplify the value created.</li>\n</ol> \n<h2><strong>Scrum Events</strong></h2> \n<p>All occasions are time-boxed occasions, with the end goal that each occasion has a maximum duration. When a Sprint starts, its span is fixed and can’t be abbreviated or extended.</p> \n<p>The remainder of the events may end at whatever point the explanation behind the event is accomplished, ensuring an appropriate proportion of time is spent without allowing waste at the same time.</p> \n<h2><strong>The Sprint</strong></h2> \n<p>The core of Scrum is a Sprint, a time-box of one month or less during which a “Done”, usable, and possibly releasable product Increment is made.</p> \n<ol>\n <li><strong>Sprint Planning:- </strong>&nbsp;A time-boxed event that occurs at the beginning of every sprint where the team determines the product backlog items they will work on during the sprint.</li>\n <li><strong>Daily Scrum:-</strong> It’s a brief time-boxed occasion for the development group to synchronize exercises and make an arrangement for the following 24 hours.</li>\n <li><strong>Sprint Review:- </strong>This is again a time-boxed event that occurs at the end of every sprint to inspect the increment and adapt the product backlog if needed.</li>\n <li><strong>Sprint Retrospective:-</strong> This occasion gives a chance to the team to review itself and make an arrangement for enhancements to be done in the following sprint</li>\n</ol> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image2.gif\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113302\" />\n</figure> \n<h2><strong>Scrum Artifacts</strong></h2> \n<p>Scrum Artifacts speak to work or incentive to give transparency and chances to investigation and transformation. Artifacts have been planned with a reason that everyone has a similar comprehension of the artifact.</p> \n<ol>\n <li><strong>Product Backlog:-</strong> An arranged rundown of everything that may be required in the product which is the single wellspring of necessities for any progressions to be made to the item. The Product Owner is liable for the Product Backlog, including its content, accessibility, and ordering.</li>\n <li><strong>Sprint Backlog:-</strong> The arrangement of Product Backlog things chose for the Sprint alongside an arrangement for conveying the item increase and understanding the run objective.</li>\n <li><strong>Product Increment:-</strong> The whole of all the Product Backlog things finished during a Sprint and the estimation of the additions of every past Sprint is called item increase.&nbsp;</li>\n <li><strong>Product Backlog Refinement:-</strong> The ongoing product backlog refinement takes place within each sprint to refine items to be ready for future sprints.</li>\n</ol> \n<h2><strong>Scrum Values</strong></h2> \n<ol>\n <li><strong>Commitment:-</strong> It is a team activity where you and your team are accountable to work together and confirm your team commitments. The scrum teams must be committed to progress and stick to the goal of the project.</li>\n <li><strong>Focus:-</strong> Once the requirements are clear and the target is set, one should be goal-oriented which motivates you for delivering faster and better.</li>\n <li><strong>Openness:-</strong> Colleagues ought to be open about their work, progress, what they realized and the issues they are confronting. Additionally, you ought to be available to work with partners, perceiving people to be people, and not resources, robots, or replaceable bits of equipment.</li>\n <li><strong>Respect:-</strong> As a piece of the Scrum group, you should regard partners, their choices, and their experience. You should regard your partners by not building anything in which individuals are not intrigued. You have to similarly regard your clients by settling their issues.</li>\n</ol> \n<p><strong>Courage:-</strong> Flexibility to change shapes the bedrock of any Scrum project and to acknowledge a change, fearlessness is required. Scrum is tied in with facing challenges and discovering an improved arrangement. The Scrum group is permitted to consider various ways to deal with the workshop the best and most proper arrangements. So as to execute new things to the undertaking, we have to disclose these new plans to the group for which you would require fearlessness.</p> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image3.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113304\" />\n</figure> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<p><em>Photo by </em><a Sethi","articleImgCdnMap":{"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/glenn-carstens-peters-RLw-UC03Gwc-unsplash-1024x681.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn81@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-38-906_f2e8211a7e959893.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image4.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx18/cdn46@2020_1/2020/08/24/15-51-41-791_08dcfe43b31f4222.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image5-2.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx4/cdn49@2020_2/2020/08/24/15-51-46-066_af10ae049da736a4.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image1-3.png":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx25/cdn33@2020_1/2020/08/24/15-51-47-719_c4708c73a6cd0e9a.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image2.gif":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx5oss/cdn45@2020_2/2020/08/24/15-51-40-821_17b43df41b9b79e8.webp","https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/image3.jpg":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx10/cdn1@2020_4/2020/08/24/15-51-41-658_c8a9979fbc7e34ea.webp","https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-post-id=113299":"https://cdn.jsdelivr.net/gh/myreaderx14/cdn13@2020_5/2020/08/24/15-51-45-695_3d9d4f0df9aada3e.webp"},"publishedOrCreatedDate":1598284297212},{"createdTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","updatedTime":"2020-08-24 23:51:37","title":"How to Market Yourself as a Freelance Software Developer","link":"https://www.noupe.com/?p=113101","description":"<div>\n <img width=\"1024\" height=\"768\" src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/per-loov-_1Z4zsEXUSk-unsplash-1024x768.jpg\" class=\"attachment-large size-large wp-post-image\" alt=\"\" style=\"margin-bottom: 15px;\" />\n</div> \n<p class=\"opener\">Software Developer is one of the fastest-growing professions. <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cuYmxzLmdvdi9vb2gvY29tcHV0ZXItYW5kLWluZm9ybWF0aW9uLXRlY2hub2xvZ3kvc29mdHdhcmUtZGV2ZWxvcGVycy5odG0%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113101\">According to the Bureau of Labor Statistics (BLS)</a>, this occupation is expected to grow by 21 percent between 2018 and 2028, which is much higher than the average job.</p> \n<p>The reason for this is simple – every industry is in need of software solutions and people who can help implement them.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>At the same time, the number of people who are turning to freelance is also growing. In 2019, <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cud2Vic2l0ZXBsYW5ldC5jb20vYmxvZy9mcmVlbGFuY2Utc3RhdHMv&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113101\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">35% of Americans were working as freelancers</a>, up by 7 percent since 2013. 28% of Americans were doing this full-time, which is up by 17% from 2014.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>All this to say, if you’re interested in becoming a freelance software developer, you’ve chosen an interesting time to do it. Demand is high for software developers, but you’ll also have plenty of competition in the freelancing space. To succeed, you’ll need to market yourself effectively and stand out from the crowd.</p> \n<h2>Identify Your Audience</h2> \n<p>The first thing you’ll want to do is narrow down your audience. As a software developer, you could work for practically any industry. However, if you try to market yourself to all of them, you’ll have a harder time making a name for yourself. Instead, you should focus on a specific niche and build your marketing strategy around them.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>There are a few things you can do to narrow down your audience. First, look at your past clients if you have any. In what niches have you produced your best work? Having some strong examples of your past work in a niche will give your marketing efforts an immediate boost.</p> \n<p>You can also think about where your own interests lie. What are your own passions? For example, if you’re someone who likes to spend your free time at the gym, the audience you target could be businesses in the health and wellness industry. By targeting an audience you’re familiar with, you’ll be able to speak their language and you’ll have more passion for the projects.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Change Your Mindset</h2> \n<p>The next thing to work on is changing your mindset. Too many freelancers find themselves in an employee mindset. The result is that they end up taking any work they can get at any price. When you’re a freelancer though, you’re not an employee – you are your own business.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>When you think about your relationship with your clients, do you find yourself thinking that you work “for” them or “with” them? If it’s the former, you’ll want to shift your mindset to the latter. Start thinking of yourself as a business that is offering its services to another business. You should focus on changing your mindset from the start, as it will end up impacting how you market yourself to the world in the subtlest of ways.&nbsp;</p> \n<h2>Establish Your Credentials</h2> \n<p>Credentials are a big reason why anyone will hire you. Most businesses won’t take a chance on freelancers who cannot demonstrate their expertise, especially when it comes to large and important projects like software development. Working as a freelancer is all about establishing trust with prospective clients, and to do this you need to have some credentials.</p> \n<p>Start with your professional credentials. If you have a degree in software development, you’re off to a great start. Another thing you can get is certifications related to software development – <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9jb21wdXRlcnNjaWVuY2Vtcy5jb20vcmVzb3VyY2VzL2NvbXB1dGVyLXNjaWVuY2UvdG9wLWNlcnRpZmljYXRpb25zLWZvci1kZXZlbG9wZXJzLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113101\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">here are some good ones to consider</a>. Other things you can use as professional credentials are previous customer testimonials and examples of your work. The more evidence you can provide of your software development proficiency, the better.</p> \n<p>After that, focus on your personal credentials. Landing clients is about more than having a good resume. You also need to be someone that your clients enjoy working with. In every interaction with your audience – including emails, your website, and social media – you need to display your positive, authoritative, and trustworthy personality. When you’re responding to an email from, or on the phone with, a potential client it may not feel like you’re still marketing yourself, but you are.</p> \n<h2>Create an Online Presence</h2> \n<p>With all of this groundwork laid, now it’s time to create your online presence. It will do a lot of marketing for you, so you should give it plenty of attention.&nbsp;</p> \n<h3>A Website</h3> \n<p>The most obvious place to start is with a website. A website is where prospective clients can come to learn about you and where you can display your best, most professional self.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Unless you’re an excellent web designer, hire someone to create a website for you. If money is tight, look for some <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cubmFtZXNpbG8uY29tLw%3D%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113101\">cheap domain names</a> to help offset the cost. A great website goes a long way though, so put as much into it as you can.</p> \n<h3>Social Media</h3> \n<p>Besides a website, you’ll also want a strong <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/social-media/social-media-presence.html\">social media presence</a>. You should have accounts on the largest social media sites, including Facebook, Twitter, and LinkedIn. Once you’re set up, make sure you use these accounts regularly. Always act professional, but allow your personality to shine through as well. Talk about things related to your niche and showcase your latest work. When someone finds your social media profile, this will be their first impression of you, so make it a good one.</p> \n<h3>Freelancing Websites</h3> \n<p>Lastly, you can establish yourself on freelancing websites. You can use sites like Upwork or Freelancer to create a professional profile and find clients who might need your services. You can also use sites that are specifically for finding software developers, such as Codementor. By creating an account on Codementor you can begin to attract some clients when you’re first starting out and build out your profile. For more information on this site, you can read this <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cDovL3d3dy5sYW5jZXJyZXZpZXcuY29tL3Jldmlldy9jb2RlbWVudG9y&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113101\">Codementor review</a>.</p> \n<h2>Make Connections</h2> \n<p>Finally, you should focus on making connections with others, and here are a few easy ways to do this:</p> \n<ul>\n <li>Look for networking events in your area where your audience might be attending</li>\n <li>Find some online groups you can join to discuss software development or the niche you’re targeting</li>\n <li>Whenever you meet someone new, be sure to mention what it is you do for a living</li>\n <li>Ask past or current clients to refer you to anyone looking for a software developer</li>\n</ul> \n<figure class=\"wp-block-image\">\n <img src=\"https://www.noupe.com/wp-content/uploads/2020/08/unsplash-7rXu_HJO9D8-unsplash-1024x683.jpg\" alt=\"\" class=\"wp-image-113106\" />\n</figure> \n<p>You’d be surprised at how much work can come your way just by making a simple connection with someone. <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/business-online/word-of-mouth.html\">Word of mouth</a> and previous clients combine for <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly93d3cud2Vic2l0ZXBsYW5ldC5jb20vYmxvZy9mcmVlbGFuY2Utc3RhdHM%3D&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113101\" rel=\"nofollow noopener\">79 percent</a> of how most freelancers find new work, so start connecting with as many new people as you can.</p> \n<p>Once you make these connections, you’ll need to nurture them. Everyone you meet won’t be ready to become a client 10 minutes later. The best thing you can do is simply let everyone know what value you provide, then let them come to you. If you are too pushy with your sales tactics, it will likely turn people away. <a href=\"https://www.noupe.com/?feed-stats-url=aHR0cHM6Ly9ibG9nLmh1YnNwb3QuY29tL21hcmtldGluZy83LWVmZmVjdGl2ZS1sZWFkLW51cnR1cmluZy10YWN0aWNz&amp;feed-stats-url-post-id=113101\">This guide</a> provides some additional tips on how you can nurture your leads.</p> \n<h2>Get Started with Your Freelance Software Developer Career</h2> \n<p>A lot of freelancers hate the marketing aspect of their business. This often happens because they are not doing it right. When done correctly, marketing yourself should be an enjoyable experience, as it allows you to make meaningful connections and help others using your skills and experience.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>Both the need for software developers and the popularity of working as a freelancer will continue to rise in the coming years. If this is something you’ve been considering, there’s no better time than the present. Start laying a solid foundation by picking your target audience and changing your mindset.&nbsp;</p> \n<p>After that, it’s just a matter of making connections and showcasing your unique strengths. It may take some time for your marketing strategy to pick up steam, but once in place, you’ll have more clients than you know what to do with.</p> \n<hr class=\"wp-block-separator\" /> \n<p><em>Photo
